### [157] [Stop Means Stop: Measuring and Repairing the Enforcement Gap in Agent-Framework Control Primitives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14166)
*Sajjad Khan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 六个主流 LLM agent 框架均存在控制原语语义泄露（审批门控期间兄弟分支、重放、取消遗留、超时僵尸等漏洞），作者设计了 Rust 实现的 SOUNDGATE 外部效应门控系统，通过内核强制路由和形式化验证，在1ms延迟和12k-26k吞吐下完全阻断所有漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示当前 LLM agent 框架中声称的屏障语义（审批暂停/取消/超时）与实际实现存在严重不一致，导致安全漏洞（兄弟分支泄露、重放执行、取消遗留、超时僵尸）并可被前沿模型实际触发。

Method: 1) 无模型差分探针方法系统测试六个框架，定位四类漏洞；2) 设计 SOUNDGATE——Rust 实现的、位于环境外部的效应门控系统，所有副作用通过内核路由强制经过；3) 使用 Verus、TLA+/TLC、TLAPS 验证核心模型，Loom 模型检查部署代码，并通过 1.2e7 操作差分一致性测试桥接模型与代码。

Result: 六个框架均存在控制语义泄露；前沿模型在固定协议下生成触发计划达14%；真实运行中215/1200次在暂停期间执行效应；SOUNDGATE 完全阻断所有漏洞，写入延迟约1ms，吞吐12k-26k次/秒。

Conclusion: 现有 LLM agent 框架的安全控制原语不可靠，需要外部强制门控机制。SOUNDGATE 提供了可验证的解决方案，但模型与代码间的保证仍为细化证据而非机械证明。

Abstract: Production LLM-agent frameworks expose control primitives -- human-in-the-loop approval gates, run cancellation, and execution timeouts -- whose names and documentation imply barrier semantics: while a run is paused, cancelled, or timed out, no gated side effect executes. We show this implied contract holds on none of the six widely used open-source frameworks we test. Model-free differential probes isolate a recurring sibling leak -- an approval gate suspends its own branch while a sibling branch's effect executes during the pause, so a later rejection cannot prevent it -- in every framework shipping a pre-execution gate (five of six), plus three further gaps: replay double-execution, cancellation orphans, and timeout zombies. The hazard is reachable, not merely constructible: under an a-priori-fixed protocol, frontier models emit the leak-triggering plan shape at pooled rates up to 14%, and when live models drive the unmodified frameworks under an approval pause, 215 of 1,200 runs execute their effect during the pause, across three schedulers and two language runtimes. To repair the measured gaps we present SOUNDGATE, an environment-external effect gate in Rust through which every side effect must be admitted, enforcing hold-until-decided, reject-cancels, dedup-on-replay, and fence-on-cancel -- one property per violation class -- under a stated complete-mediation contract discharged for network egress by kernel-enforced routes. We verify the properties over a model of the admission core (Verus; TLA+/TLC, exhaustive to 7.5e7 states; TLAPS), model-check the deployed Rust with Loom, and bridge model to code by differential conformance over 1.2e7 operations -- refinement evidence, not a mechanized proof. SOUNDGATE blocks every measured violation end-to-end on all six frameworks while releasing legitimate effects, at about 1 ms admission per write and 12k-26k durable admissions per second.

</details>


### [158] [Structured Feedback Improves Repair in an LLM Agent Loop](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14167)
*Jaideep Ray,Ankit Goyal*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出VeriHarness框架，通过代码控制智能体循环，让LLM生成候选方案并由外部验证器控制接受、预算和追踪。实验发现，包含失败位置、观测值和可接受替代方案的完整反馈，能显著提升任务成功率（Qwen2.5-Coder-14B提高44个百分点，Llama-3.1-8B提高42个百分点），且增益主要来自可接受替代方案信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在外部验证拒绝后重新尝试时，验证与模型调用之间的接口缺乏明确定义，缺少对反馈信息如何影响模型修复效果的系统研究。

Method: 提出VeriHarness代码控制智能体循环框架，模型生成候选方案，外部验证器控制接受、预算和追踪。在50个TextWorld游戏配对实验中，比较原始诊断与包含失败位置、观测值和可接受替代方案的结构化反馈，并设置消融实验。

Result: 完整反馈（位置+观测值+替代方案）在4次调用预算下使Qwen2.5-Coder-14B成功率从14/50提升至36/50（+44%），Llama-3.1-8B从8/50提升至29/50（+42%）。消融实验表明增益主要来自可接受替代方案信息。JSON格式与散文格式效果相当。

Conclusion: 结构化反馈中可接受替代方案信息是提升LLM智能体修复效果的关键因素，反馈格式（JSON vs 散文）对修复效果无显著影响，该结论在不同的调用预算和解码设置下保持稳定。

Abstract: LLM agents often retry after external validation rejects a candidate, but the interface between validation and the next model call remains underspecified. We introduce VeriHarness, a code-controlled agent loop in which models generate candidates while external validators control acceptance, budgets, and traces. We use it to compare raw diagnostics with feedback that identifies the failure location, observed value, and admissible alternatives. Across 50 paired TextWorld games under a four-call cap, feedback containing all three fields raises terminal success from 14/50 to 36/50 for Qwen2.5-Coder-14B (+44 percentage points) and from 8/50 to 29/50 for Llama-3.1-8B (+42 points). Ablations locate most of the gain in the admissible alternatives: feedback containing only the location and observed value remains near the raw diagnostic baseline. Presenting the complete repair information in prose instead of a keyed JSON record yields nearly the same success, providing no evidence that JSON syntax itself improves repair. The ordering persists across the tested call budgets and one sampled-decoding setting.

</details>


### [159] [Quantize with Confidence? An Empirical Study of Quantization for Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14181)
*Saima Afrin,Md. Zahidul Haque,Antonio Mastropaolo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文实证评估了六种量化方法在两种代码大模型上的影响，发现AQLM能匹配甚至超越全精度基线，而QuIP#在高复杂度提示下性能下降最显著，安全性保持稳定，提示选择量化策略时需超越功能正确性进行评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着Ollama等本地推理框架的普及，开发者在资源受限硬件上运行大型代码模型的需求增加，后训练量化虽可减少内存占用，但其对生成代码的影响尚不明确，需系统评估。

Method: 评估六种量化方法（GPTQ、AWQ、QuIP#、AQLM、BitsAndBytes、GGUF）在Qwen2.5-Coder和CodeLlama两个模型家族上的表现，使用McEval和CoderEval基准测试功能正确性（pass@1），并结合可维护性、可靠性、安全性、结构复杂度以及提示复杂度（Shannon熵和token长度）下的鲁棒性分析。

Result: AQLM表现最佳，一致匹配或超越全精度基线；QuIP#正确性下降最严重，尤其在高复杂度提示下；安全性在不同模型、基准和编程语言间保持稳定；提示复杂度鲁棒性因量化方法而异。

Conclusion: 为资源受限硬件上部署代码模型时选择量化策略提供了实用指导，强调评估量化模型时不能仅看功能正确性，还需关注代码质量和鲁棒性等多维度指标。

Abstract: The growing adoption of local inference frameworks such as Ollama has made it increasingly common for developers to run large code models on laptops and other resource-constrained hardware. In these settings, post-training quantization is essential for reducing memory footprint and enabling practical deployment, yet its impact on generated code remains insufficiently understood. We empirically evaluate six state-of-the-art quantization methods (GPTQ, AWQ, QuIP#, AQLM, BitsAndBytes, and GGUF) on two representative large code model families, Qwen2.5-Coder and CodeLlama, using the multilingual McEval and CoderEval benchmarks for Python and Java. We assess functional correctness (pass@1) together with maintainability, reliability, security, and structural complexity. We also introduce a novel analysis of robustness under varying prompt complexity, characterized by Shannon entropy and token length. Our results show that quantization techniques differ meaningfully in their impact on correctness and code quality. AQLM consistently matches or exceeds the full-precision baseline, whereas QuIP# exhibits the largest correctness degradation, particularly on complex prompts. Security attributes remain stable across models, benchmarks, and programming languages, while robustness to prompt complexity varies across techniques. These findings provide practical guidance for selecting quantization strategies for deploying large code models on resource-constrained hardware and highlight the importance of evaluating quantized models beyond functional correctness.

</details>


### [160] [NexForge: Scaling Executable Agent Tasks via Requirement-First Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14186)
*Jiarong Zhao,Zhikai Lei,Zhiheng Xi,Rui Zheng,Hang Yan,Jie Zhou,Qin Chen,Liang He*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: NexForge是一个需求优先的框架，能够将自由形式的能力需求编译成可执行的智能体训练数据，无需领域特定基础设施即可生成大量终端和办公任务，显著提升模型性能，并训练出达到开源SOTA的Nex-N2模型系列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法受限于"基板优先"范式，任务生成依赖于预定义工具、代码库或技能图谱，扩展覆盖范围需要手动扩展基板，每个新域都需要定制化流水线，且任务分布常反映基板便利性而非真实需求。

Method: 提出NexForge框架：(1) 基于研究的需求发现，识别代表性任务形式、真实场景及其相对流行度；(2) 分布感知的任务编译，自动检索或构建文件、仓库、依赖和运行时配置；(3) 教师轨迹收集与轨迹蒸馏。

Result: 同一流水线无需领域特定基础设施即可生成3,600个终端任务和2,000个办公任务；将Qwen3.5-35B-A3B Base在Terminal-Bench 2.0上从22.5%提升至52.0%，在GDPval上从813 Elo提升至1338 Elo；扩展到43.2K终端任务达到58.4%，超越Claude Opus 4.6；训练出的Nex-N2模型达到75.3%和1585 Elo，超越多个前沿专有系统。

Conclusion: NexForge展示了需求优先的数据生成范式的有效性，无需领域特定基础设施即可跨域生成高质量智能体训练数据，训练出的Nex-N2模型达到了开源SOTA性能，甚至超越多个专有前沿系统。

Abstract: Scaling executable agent training data is bottlenecked by substrate-first methods that tie task generation to predefined tools, repositories, or skill graphs: expanding coverage requires manual expansion of the substrate, each new domain demands a bespoke pipeline, and the resulting task distributions often reflect substrate convenience rather than real-world demand. We introduce NexForge, a requirement-first framework that compiles free-form capability requirements into executable agent training data. NexForge first performs research-based demand discovery to identify representative task forms, realistic scenarios, and their relative prevalence. It then applies distribution-aware task compilation and automatically retrieves or constructs the files, repositories, dependencies, and runtime configurations required to materialize each task, followed by teacher rollout collection and trajectory distillation. The same pipeline, without any domain-specific infrastructure, produces 3,600 terminal tasks and 2,000 office tasks, improving Qwen3.5-35B-A3B Base from 22.5% to 52.0% on Terminal-Bench 2.0 and from 813 to 1338 Elo on GDPval; scaling to 43.2K terminal tasks reaches 58.4%, surpassing Claude Opus 4.6. Scaled further, NexForge-synthesized data contributes to the training of Nex-N2, a family of publicly available agent models that lift Qwen3.5-35B-A3B to 75.3% on Terminal-Bench 2.1 and to 1585 Elo on GDPval -- achieving state-of-the-art open-source performance and surpassing several frontier proprietary systems. Nex-N2 models are available at https://nex.sii.edu.cn/

</details>


### [161] [ToolAlignBench: Investigating Alignment Conflicts in Tool-Calling Enabled LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14285)
*Aryan Keluskar,Amrita Bhattacharjee,Huan Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究了安全对齐的LLM在工具调用场景中，当安全价值观（如公共福利）与部署指令（如内部日志）冲突时，模型会优先遵循安全训练而非指令，导致"告密"等行为，最高43.4%的概率覆盖指令。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究安全对齐的LLM在受监管行业中处理机密文件时，安全训练引发的价值观与部署指令发生冲突时的行为选择，揭示多元对齐中的根本张力。

Method: 构建了涵盖16个领域128个场景的基准测试，评估安全对齐的开源模型在工具调用场景中面对冲突指令时的行为表现。

Result: 安全对齐的开源模型在高达43.4%的情况下会覆盖部署指令，执行告密、数据泄露和篡改证据等行为；abliteration（消除安全训练）可降低外部告密率。

Conclusion: 安全训练在保护用户的同时，可能导致模型违背部署指令，产生不可预测的 Liability 风险，揭示了多元价值观对齐中的根本性冲突。

Abstract: Safety alignment in LLMs aims to align models with human values, but which values take precedence when they conflict? We investigate this question in the context of tool-calling LLM agents deployed in regulated industries, where agents processing confidential documents may encounter content that triggers safety-trained values (e.g., public welfare) that conflict with deployment-context instructions (e.g., internal logging). To empirically verify this phenomenon, we build a benchmark of 128 scenarios across 16 domains. We find that safety-aligned open-source models override their deployment instructions up to 43.4% of the time, engaging in whistleblowing, data exfiltration, and evidence tampering when processing documents that suggest organizational wrongdoing. We also find that abliteration reduces rates of external whistleblowing. These results reveal a fundamental tension in pluralistic alignment, where the same safety training that protects users can cause agents to act against deployment instructions in ways that create unpredictable liability risks. We release our benchmark as a framework to support evaluation of agent behavior under competing legitimate interests.

</details>

### [163] [The Prover Is the Judge: Verified Security Software from AI Coding Agents in Ada/SPARK](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14340)
*Tobias Philipp*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文探讨了AI编码代理在编写和验证安全软件中的应用，提出“验证者驱动循环”方法，使用Ada/SPARK语言编写密码学、TLS 1.3、IKEv2、X.509和Matrix客户端等安全软件。GNATprove验证器成功处理了49,280个证明义务，验证了选定原语的功能正确性，并以比人工验证低20-40倍的监督成本证明了其余代码无运行时错误。但GNATprove不足以检测所有缺陷，需通过已知答案测试、互操作性测试或人工审查规范来解决。论文指出，代理可被信任的程度受其反馈强度的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI编码代理生成代码的速度远超人类审查速度，导致代码质量难以保证。本文旨在探索如何利用验证器作为“法官”来判断代码正确性，从而在高效生成代码的同时确保安全性。

Method: 采用“验证者驱动循环”方法，即AI代理编写代码后由形式验证工具（GNATprove）进行验证。若验证失败，代理根据反馈修改代码直至通过。对于GNATprove无法检测的缺陷，辅以已知答案测试、互操作性测试和人工规范审查。

Result: GNATprove成功处理49,280个证明义务，验证了功能正确性并证明无运行时错误，监督成本仅为人工验证的1/20至1/40。但GNATprove未能检测所有缺陷，需其他方法补充。代理在弱校验条件下会尝试绕过验证并报告成功。

Conclusion: AI代理可被信任的程度受其反馈强度的限制。验证器的能力越强，代理越能被信任；反之，若验证器存在盲点，代理可能利用这些盲点“作弊”。因此，强大的形式化验证反馈是确保AI代理生成安全代码的关键。

Abstract: AI coding agents produce code faster than humans can review it. In our approach, the prover is the judge of whether the code is correct. Under a verifier-driven loop, AI agents wrote and verified bare-metal security software in Ada/SPARK spanning classical and post-quantum cryptography, TLS 1.3, IKEv2, X.509, and a Matrix client. GNATprove discharged 49,280 proof obligations, established functional correctness for selected primitives, and proved the absence of run-time errors for the rest, at roughly 20-40 times lower supervision cost than comparable hand verification. GNATprove alone was insufficient: some defects could not be detected and were resolved using known-answer tests, interoperability, or human review of specifications. Given weak checks, the agent tried to bypass them and reported success. We report where each layer caught faults and draw the central lesson: what an agent can be trusted to establish is bounded by the strength of its feedback.

### [164] [Why Git Is the Memory Solution for the Agentic Development Lifecycle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14390)
*Frank Guo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于Git版本控制的代理开发生命周期（ADLC）记忆系统，将推理过程绑定到仓库版本控制中，通过种子供应（检索排序）和答案组装（路由分发）两个阶段，实现零标注成本的代码变更推理追溯，在真实开发者问题上达到0.83答案充分性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前编码代理产生的代码越来越多，但每次变更背后的推理过程（替代方案权衡、约束发现、被拒绝的方法）都困在即将消失的助手会话记录中。现有记忆系统通常被当作单一检索问题，构建为分层存储、记忆图谱、编译维基等复杂机制，但难以保证真实性和可靠性。

Method: 提出Git绑定的记忆系统，将推理过程嵌入版本控制。分两个阶段解决：1）种子供应（Seed Supply）：在8个语料库上对比5种导入排序机制，保留2种，最佳配置达~0.31 pooled MRR；2）答案组装（Answer Assembly）：使用路由器分发三种查询——广度查询走Git锚定结构图、定点查询走置信度门控的会话记录、原理查询走决策合成（重构跨会话的推理链），在~50k LOC生产系统上达0.83充分性。

Result: 种子供应阶段：最佳配置~0.31 pooled MRR，比原始会话文本grep基线高~60x，比解析后的逐轮基线高~15x。答案组装阶段：路由系统每个问题仅需382-980 tokens，比完整历史低三个数量级；决策合成在年轻生产系统上达0.83充分性；所有结果可在用户自有历史零标注成本复现。

Conclusion: 记忆不应作为独立机械系统构建，而应绑定到已有版本控制基础设施上，利用commit的真实性、rebuild的新鲜度、merge的验证性、review的约束性。当前主要约束在于捕获（capture）环节，即如何系统性地记录推理过程。

Abstract: Coding agents now produce a growing share of a team's code, while the reasoning behind each change -- the alternatives weighed, the constraints discovered, the approaches rejected -- is trapped in assistant transcripts that vanish with the session. Memory for this setting, the agentic development lifecycle (ADLC), is usually posed as one retrieval problem and built as machinery: tiered stores, memory graphs, compiled wikis, model-judged admission. We argue memory should instead be git-bound -- built into the repository's version control, inheriting the guarantees the machinery struggles to construct: ground truth from commits, freshness from rebuild, verification from the merge, containment from review. On this ledger we solve two problems separately, then combine them. Seed supply is closed as an eight-corpus retrieval study under a pre-registered ship discipline: five imported ranking mechanisms rejected, two kept, and a best configuration of ~0.31 pooled MRR -- ~60x the raw-transcript grep floor, ~15x an honest parsed-turn floor. Answer assembly is where ranking stops helping: single-shot retrieval scores only 0.07-0.20 answer-sufficiency on real developer questions, and ungated episode injection measurably degrades good answers. A router dispatches breadth to a git-anchored structural map, pointed lookups to confidence-gated episodes, and rationale to decision synthesis, which reconstructs why-arcs no single session contains (0.83 sufficiency on a young ~50k-LOC production system). Routed, the system answers at 382-980 tokens per question -- three orders of magnitude below the recorded history. Because ground truth is mined from commit-session links rather than annotated, every result is replicable on any user's own history at zero labeling cost. The remaining constraint is capture. Code, benchmark, and paper source: github.com/rekal-dev/rekal-cli.

</details>


### [165] [AI-Conducted Interviews in Empirical Software Engineering: An Experience Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14452)
*Rohit Gheyi,Danyllo Albuquerque,Márcio Ribeiro,Mirko Perkusich*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文报告了在两项实证软件工程研究中使用定制版MyGPT进行半结构化AI访谈的经验。66份提交的分析显示，92.4%符合预期格式，参与者普遍给予正面评价（90.9%整体体验积极，95.5%认为问题清晰等），但存在问题深度不足、隐私顾虑等局限。AI访谈应作为人工访谈的补充选项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 定制MyGPT进行自管理式短访谈，包含语音交互、多语言支持、预设协议和结构化合成报告。在两个ESE研究（重构实践和Scrum中生成式AI应用）中部署，分析66份提交物和问卷反馈。

Conclusion: AI访谈在工作流可行性和可接受性上得到支持，但不能替代完成率、时间节省、忠实度等方面的评估。应作为短期、聚焦、低风险研究的补充工具，需注意协议设计、隐私指导、人工验证和人工监督。

Abstract: Semi-structured interviews are widely used in empirical software engineering (ESE), but they are resource-intensive and difficult to coordinate across schedules, locations, and natural languages. This experience report examines a customized MyGPT used to conduct short, self-administered interviews in two ESE studies: one on refactoring practices and another on generative AI in Scrum-related activities. Participants accessed the interviewer through shared links, used voice interaction, selected a preferred natural language, and completed the interview without a researcher present. The AI followed a predefined protocol and generated a structured synthesis that participants voluntarily submitted; these artifacts were not treated as verbatim transcripts. We analyzed 66 submissions and questionnaire responses, and audited artifact format, language, length, and protocol consistency. Of the submitted artifacts, 92.4% followed the expected synthesis format, 65 were predominantly in Portuguese and one in English, and two conflicted with the reported protocol. Participants generally rated the experience positively: 90.9% reported a positive overall experience and comfort, 95.5% considered the questions clear, 97.0% rated the pace positively, and 89.4% would participate again. Reported limitations included generic questions, limited sensitivity to answers, insufficient depth, privacy concerns, and missed human interaction. The findings support the operational viability and acceptability of this workflow among analyzed respondents, but do not establish completion rates, time savings, summary fidelity, or equivalence to human-conducted interviews. AI interviewers should therefore be treated as a complementary option for short, focused, low-risk studies, with protocol design, privacy guidance, artifact validation, and human oversight.

  <summary>Details</summary>

We investigate this question in the context of business process automation, focusing on the transformation of Business Process Model and Notation (BPMN) diagrams into executable agentic workflows. Since BPMN specifies explicit control-flow semantics, we focus on deterministic workflows in which a fixed process model and inputs uniquely determine the executed path. We introduce a specialist workflow for this task and compare it against generalist agents such as Roo and Cline. Our results show that the specialist solution produces agents that outperform generalist baselines by approximately 9-20 percentage points in tool-use exactness, 2-4x in penalty-adjusted latency, and 3x fewer tool-call errors, while reducing generation token cost by over 95% and eliminating repair iterations. Abstract: This paper presents a computational model to predict human visual attention over words in software source code. We propose a model of programmer visual attention in which we design a novel loss function that computes similarity between human attention measured during eye tracking experiments and the internal attention of the artificial neural network. Our model outperforms the baseline in software engineering by 64%, 16%, and 467% in each of these studies according to Pearson correlation. We used scanpath prediction as an example to demonstrate that our model is more capable of the task that requires the understanding of human thought process. ### [168] [A Deterministic Binary Fingerprinting Framework with Zero-Trained Feature Extraction for Sparse Count Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14596)
*Lei Zhao,Fujin Huang,Ling Kang,Quan Guo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: MMTB是一种无需训练、基于二值化的确定性表示框架，通过列式Min-Max归一化和固定阈值将单细胞转录组等稀疏计数数据映射为温湿度计指纹，使用汉明距离进行聚类，在粗粒度任务上接近PCA+Leiden效果，内存减少约10倍，但细粒度区分能力不如连续嵌入方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的单细胞转录组数据分析依赖PCA降维、图聚类或连续嵌入空间的迭代优化，计算和存储成本较高。作者希望设计一种无需监督、无需模型训练、无需梯度优化的轻量级二值化表示方法，以降低资源需求，适用于粗粒度分离和资源受限的场景。

Method: 提出MMTB框架：对列进行Min-Max归一化，采用固定阈值将每个样本映射为温湿度计指纹（thermometer fingerprint），得到固定宽度的二值编码。使用汉明距离计算样本间相似度，并基于汉明最近邻图+Leiden算法进行聚类。还提供了一个无标签的适用性评分作为部署指南。

Result: 经验上，汉明距离与归一化L1距离的Pearson相关系数约0.92。在三细胞系混合数据上，3阈值指纹的NMI达0.99，每个细胞仅188字节。在粗粒度任务上接近PCA+Leiden。但在精细注释任务（如PBMC）上，NMI为0.39（Scanpy为0.49），表明细粒度区分能力有限。内存相比float32减少约10倍。

Conclusion: MMTB适用于粗粒度分离和资源受限的部署场景，不适合细粒度亚型发现或作为连续嵌入的通用替代。作者明确不声称通用压缩优势（PCA30和稀疏CSR可能更小），并提供了适用性评分作为部署参考。

Abstract: Sparse count matrices from single-cell transcriptomes to k-mer profiles and document-term frequencies are conventionally analyzed via PCA-reduced graph clustering or iterative optimization in continuous embedding spaces. We introduce MMTB, a deterministic non-learned binary representation framework that requires no label supervision, model fitting, or gradient-based optimization. Column-wise Min-Max normalization followed by fixed cutoffs maps each sample to a thermometer fingerprint whose Hamming distances show empirical correspondence with normalized L1 distances, with Pearson correlation approximately 0.92 on single-cell RNA-seq pairs. In a favorable three-cell-line mixture, the 3-threshold fingerprint achieves NMI of 0.99 at 188 bytes per cell. Under a fair Hamming nearest-neighbor graph plus Leiden readout, MMTB approaches PCA plus Leiden on this coarse task. On challenging tissue-like annotations, continuous pipelines often lead; PBMC Seurat NMI is 0.39 for MMTB versus 0.49 for Scanpy, underscoring that MMTB is suited for coarse-grained separation and resource-constrained deployments rather than fine-grained subtype discovery or as a general replacement for continuous embeddings. Relative to dense float32 representations, MMTB fingerprints reduce memory by approximately 10-fold while providing fixed-width Hamming-indexable codes. PCA30 embeddings and sparse CSR may be smaller; we do not claim universal compression. A label-free suitability score is provided as a deployment guideline, not a performance predictor.

### [169] [SYNAPSE: A Multi-LLM Orchestrated AI Tutor for Secure Software Development Education with Neurodivergent-First Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14601)
*Giusy Ferrara,Ashkan Sami*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SYNAPSE是一个自适应编程辅导平台，集成了Claude、GPT-4o和Gemini三大模型，面向Java、Python网络安全和安全软件开发教学。该平台具有18项无障碍功能，并通过一个故意存在漏洞的Web应用ShopSecure（覆盖OWASP Top 10 2021六大类别）训练学习者检测-理解-修复的漏洞维护循环。19名参与者的可行性试验显示系统可用性得分76.4，参与度4.2/5，神经多样性与神经典型人群认知负荷相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全软件开发教育仅在学习编程基础后才教授，而ADHD及执行功能差异学习者的需求未被充分关注。研究者希望开发一个同时兼顾安全技能训练和无障碍需求的平台，让学习者在真实维护场景中练习"检测-理解-修复"的漏洞修复循环。

Method: SYNAPSE通过Model Context Protocol协调Claude、GPT-4o和Gemini三个大模型，依据教学意图在三阶段苏格拉底式提示策略下路由交互；提供18项始终可见的无障碍功能；以ShopSecure（映射OWASP Top 10 2021中六大类别）为实践靶场，让学习者练习漏洞发现与修复。

Result: 19名参与者（涵盖神经多样性与神经典型人群）的可行性试验显示：系统可用性量表得分76.4，参与度评分4.2/5，且两个群体的认知负荷水平相当。

Conclusion: SYNAPSE在安全软件开发教育中展现出良好的可用性和包容性，能够同时服务于神经多样性和神经典型学习者，为自适应安全编程教育提供了可行的技术方案。

Abstract: Developers who maintain real systems must continually recognise and remediate vulnerabilities in existing code, yet this skill is rarely trained directly: secure software development is commonly taught only after programming fluency is acquired, and accessibility support is treated as a secondary concern, disadvantaging learners with ADHD and related executive-function differences. This paper presents SYNAPSE, a publicly deployed adaptive tutoring platform for Java, Python for cybersecurity, and secure software development. SYNAPSE coordinates Claude, GPT-4o, and Gemini through the Model Context Protocol, routing interactions by pedagogical intent under a three-stage Socratic hint policy. It exposes eighteen always-visible accessibility features and anchors practice in ShopSecure, a deliberately vulnerable web application mapped to six OWASP Top 10 (2021) categories, on which learners practise the detect-understand-remediate loop characteristic of software maintenance. A feasibility pilot with nineteen participants across neurodivergent and neurotypical cohorts returned a System Usability Scale score of 76.4 and engagement of 4.2/5, with comparable cognitive-load levels across cohorts. SYNAPSE is available at https://synapse-course.com; a screencast is available at https://youtu.be/9R17KC47qQI.

Abstract: We advocate for AI/ML issue resolution frameworks tailored to maintenance workflows and the nature of modern AI/ML systems. To identify the unique characteristics of issue resolution in AI/ML systems and motivate the need for tailored frameworks, we conducted a qualitative study of issue resolution workflows documented in 100 issue reports and pull requests across four widely used AI/ML systems: TensorFlow, scikit-learn, MLflow, and AutoGPT. ### [172] [Large Language Models for Code Generation from Multilingual Prompts: A Curated Benchmark and a Study on Code Quality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14816)
*Saima Afrin,Alessandro Midolo,Camilo Escobar-Velásquez,Mario Linares-Vásquez,Weiyuan Ding,Bowen Xu,Massimiliano Di Penta,Antonio Mastropaolo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究不同自然语言提示对LLM生成代码质量的影响，发现英语并非始终最优，且影响取决于编程语言和模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然自然语言提示影响LLM文本生成（语言偏差）已被广泛研究，但这种偏差对代码生成质量和编程惯例的影响尚未被充分探索。

Method: 构建460个编程任务（Python 230个，Java 230个），将英文提示翻译并人工审校为中文、印地语、西班牙语和意大利语，评估GPT-4o mini、DeepSeek、Claude生成代码的功能正确性、结构质量、静态分析问题和词法特征。

Result: (i) 英语并非始终产生最佳结果；(ii) 提示语言的影响因编程语言和LLM而异；(iii) 生成的代码经常在注释和字符串字面量中混合英语和提示语言。

Conclusion: 提供了首个用于研究代码生成语言偏差的多语言基准，为开发更鲁棒的多语言代码生成系统提供了见解。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) perform differently on identical programming tasks when prompted in different natural languages, a phenomenon known as language bias. While this behavior has been widely studied for general text generation, its impact on code generation quality and programming conventions remains largely unexplored. We investigate how the language used to describe programming tasks affects the source code generated by GPT-4o mini, DeepSeek, and Claude. Our study comprises 460 coding tasks spanning Python (230) and Java (230). We translate and manually curate the original English prompts into Chinese, Hindi, Spanish, and Italian while preserving their technical meaning. We evaluate the generated code using multiple dimensions, including functional correctness through test pass rates, structural quality using established code metrics, issues detected by static analysis tools, and lexical characteristics such as the language used in identifiers and comments. Our results show that (i) English prompts do not consistently produce the best functional correctness or code quality, (ii) the impact of prompt language depends on both the programming language and the LLM, and (iii) generated code frequently mixes English with the prompt language in comments and string literals. These findings provide the first curated multilingual benchmark for studying language bias in code generation and offer insights for developing more robust multilingual code generation systems.

Method: 基于分解与RAG流水线：1) 自然语言描述被分解为离散GUI特征；2) 从32个基础组件的自定义库中检索匹配组件；3) 以Figma自动布局渲染为可编辑图层。采用Gemini 2.5 Flash作为LLM后端，Node.js/Express提供服务，并引入人工审核编辑步骤。

We present AI Prototyper, an open-source Figma plugin that automates GUI prototyping through a decomposition and retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) pipeline. Given a natural-language description of a desired screen, such as a login page or a product detail card, the plugin decomposes the request into discrete GUI features, retrieves matching components from a custom 32-primitive library, and renders each component as a fully editable Figma layer with auto-layout. The pipeline uses Gemini 2.5 Flash as its LLM back-end and a Node.js/Express service. Unlike existing decomposition-based tools, AI Prototyper introduces a human-in-the-loop editing step that lets users review, modify, or extend the generated feature list before rendering, uses a different technology stack and LLM family, and supports multilingual input, producing correctly labelled interfaces in Thai, English, and Mandarin Chinese. In a preliminary evaluation, participants using AI Prototyper completed more prototypes in a fixed time window than those working manually, and expert practitioners rated the AI-generated prototypes higher across nine quality dimensions. A demonstration video is available at https://youtu.be/pRoFAH7MQaE. The source code and component library are available at https://github.com/tongsalangsingha/AI-prototyper-tool

### [174] [StructureClaw: Traceable LLM Agents and an Executable Benchmark for Structural Engineering Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14896)
*Sizhong Qin,Yi Gu,Yao Jiang,Ao Cai,Changjian Zhou,Shaoxuan Shuai,Jiachang Wang,Tianhao Shen,Yueqiang Li,Xinhao Li,Li Zeng,Yueshi Chen,Dachen Gao,Genrong Xu,Wenjie Liao,Xinzheng Lu*

TL;DR: 本文提出 StructureClaw，一个以工件为中心的工程智能体工作台，以及 StructureClaw-Bench 基准测试。在150个结构化工程场景中，通过完整的工件链验证（而非仅最终答案），将平均成功率从56.8%提升至88.6%，揭示了交互式和多模态重建中的关键挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估聚焦于问答或脚本生成，无法验证结构工程中所需的完整证据链（解释需求、计算模型、验证记录、求解器输出、代码检查记录和最终报告），导致即使输出流畅但底层工作流不完整、不一致或不可执行也可能获得高分。

Method: 构建 StructureClaw 工作台，LLM 代理通过受控工程技能、类型化工具、共享工件状态和本地分析后端运行；同时构建 StructureClaw-Bench 基准，包含150个控制场景（标准工作流执行、交互鲁棒性、多模态结构模型重建），仅当所有工件和执行层面的断言一次通过才算成功。

Result: 在10种代理-模型配置、50个标准案例上，平均成功率从通用技能基线的56.8%提升至全自动工作流的88.6%。交互式和多模态评估识别出两个主要挑战：安全处理无效数值输入、以及保持构件一致性的结构模型重建。

Conclusion: 以工件为中心的评估能够暴露从最终回答中难以发现的工作流层面失败，为评估和改进结构工程智能体提供了更严格的基准。

Abstract: Addressing a structural-engineering request requires more than a single answer; it requires a chain of interdependent artifacts: interpreted requirements, a computable model, validation records, solver outputs, code-check records, and a final report. Evaluations centered on question answering or script generation rarely verify this complete evidence chain and may therefore reward fluent outputs even when the underlying engineering workflow is incomplete, internally inconsistent, or non-executable. To address this limitation, we present StructureClaw, an artifact-centered workbench in which LLM agents operate through governed engineering skills, typed tools, shared artifact state, and local analysis backends. We also introduce StructureClaw-Bench, an executable benchmark of 150 controlled scenarios spanning standard workflow execution, interactive robustness, and multimodal structural-model reconstruction. A scenario succeeds only when all required artifact- and execution-level assertions pass in a single run. Across ten agent-model configurations, each evaluated on the same 50 standard cases, the average Success Rate rises from 56.8% with the generic-skill baseline to 88.6% with the full automatic workflow. The interactive and multimodal evaluations identify two prominent remaining challenges: safe handling of invalid numerical inputs and fixture-consistent reconstruction of structural models. These findings show that artifact-centered evaluation can expose workflow-level failures that are difficult to identify from final responses alone, providing a more rigorous basis for evaluating and improving structural-engineering agents. The code and benchmark are available at https://github.com/structureclaw/structureclaw.

### [175] [FirmPilot: Evidence-Guided Multi-Agent Environment Recovery for IoT Firmware Rehosting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14903)
*Yanbing Shen,Fan Zhang,Haitao Xu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: FirmPilot是一个基于证据引导的多智能体框架，通过迭代环境重建、搜索决策、执行规划与专用智能体协同，显著提升固件重托管中Web服务与网络可达性，优于现有方法FirmAE。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有固件重托管方法在面对多样化真实固件时脆弱性高，模板驱动框架难以适配长尾厂商规范，而大语言模型的无约束使用可能导致不可支持的修改与不可复现的执行。

Method: 提出FirmPilot多智能体框架，包含搜索智能体（基于相似性检索）、规划智能体（协调执行可接受的转换）和专用智能体（恢复文件系统/init产物、持久化状态与网络暴露），通过反复执行与证据驱动的产物差异解决跨层依赖。

Result: 在LFwC固件语料库上，FirmPilot将Web服务可达性从25.49%提升至52.39%，网络可达性从39.30%提升至71.93%；每固件平均检测服务数从0.86增至1.62，并支持RouterSploit交互与协议感知模糊测试等下流分析。

Conclusion: 证据与反馈驱动的智能体协调能够有效提升固件自动重托管的成功率、服务恢复能力与下流实用性。

Abstract: Firmware rehosting executes firmware images in emulated environments such as QEMU to enable scalable dynamic analysis of Internet of Things (IoT) devices. In practice, rehosting pipelines remain fragile across diverse real-world firmware images, as reaching an externally observable execution state depends on tightly coupled artifacts spanning boot scripts, persistent configuration (e.g., NVRAM-like key-value state), and network setup. Template-driven frameworks often fail to accommodate long-tail vendor conventions, while unconstrained use of large language models (LLMs) risks unsupported modifications and irreproducible executions. We introduce FirmPilot, an evidence-guided multi-agent framework for environment recovery in firmware rehosting. FirmPilot reformulates rehosting as iterative environment reconstruction in which a search agent grounds decisions through similarity-based retrieval, a planner coordinates execution-accepted transitions, and specialized agents recover filesystem/init artifacts, persistent state, and network exposure. Through repeated execution and evidence-grounded artifact deltas, the system resolves cross-layer dependencies across boot, state, and networking that otherwise prevent firmware executions from reaching a stable, externally reachable state in emulation. Evaluated on the large-scale, real-world LFwC firmware corpus, FirmPilot improves web-service reachability over FirmAE from 25.49% to 52.39% and network reachability from 39.30% to 71.93%. The resulting rehosts raise the average number of detected services per firmware from 0.86 to 1.62 and support downstream analysis workflows, including RouterSploit interaction and protocol-aware fuzzing over recovered service surfaces. The evaluation shows that evidence- and feedback-grounded agent coordination improves rehosting success, service recovery, and downstream utility in automated firmware rehosting.

### [176] [Leaf: An Instrumentation-based Dynamic Analysis Framework for Rust](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15025)
*Mohammad Omidvar Tehrani,Marco Gaboardi,Nick Sumner,Steven Y. Ko*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了LEAF，一个基于插桩的Rust动态分析框架。它通过捕获MIR级别的语义信息并增强运行时事实，以事件流形式提供给分析任务。三个案例（符号执行器、Rust专用消毒器、控制流追踪器）验证了其实用性，编译和运行时开销可控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Rust语言发展迅速，但缺乏一个通用的动态分析框架。现有工具无法充分利用Rust丰富的语义信息（所有权模型、类型系统、内存模型、编译器级表示），LEAF旨在填补这一空白，将Rust特有的语义信息提供给动态分析。

Method: LEAF是一个基于插桩的动态分析框架，核心是捕获MIR（中间表示）级别的语义信息，结合运行时事实，通过名为Dynamic MIR（DMIR）的事件驱动编程接口，以事件流形式将分析信息传递给上层分析任务。

Result: 通过三个实质性动态分析任务（混合符号执行器、Rust专用消毒器、控制流追踪器）验证了LEAF的实用性和表现力。评估表明其编译和运行时开销在可接受范围内。

Conclusion: LEAF成功填补了Rust生态中通用动态分析框架的空白，能够有效利用Rust丰富的语义信息支持多种分析任务，且开销可控，具有较好的实用价值。

Abstract: This paper presents LEAF, an instrumentation-based dynamic analysis framework for Rust. Although Rust has grown rapidly in recent years, the landscape of program analysis tools for Rust is still in relatively early stages. One notable gap is the lack of a general-purpose dynamic analysis framework that can support different analysis tasks. LEAF aims to fill this gap by providing a Rust-native framework for analyzing Rust programs at runtime. Rust provides rich semantic information through its ownership model, type system, memory model, and compiler-level representation. Therefore, LEAF focuses on how to make this information available to dynamic analyses. In particular, LEAF captures MIR-level semantic information, augments it with runtime facts, and delivers it to analyses as an event stream through Dynamic MIR (DMIR), an event-driven programming interface. Through three substantial dynamic analyses -- a concolic executor, a Rust-specific sanitizer, and a control-flow tracer -- we demonstrate the practicality and expressiveness of LEAF. Our evaluation further shows that LEAF's compile-time and runtime overhead is meaningful but manageable.

Our approach leverages Software Product Line (SPL) engineering principles, treating design patterns as configurable assets within a product line and supporting automated generation of custom design patterns. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子计算环境由异构层级（硬件、软件开发工具包、应用）组成，从业者面对碎片化且快速演变的生态，缺乏系统性的指导原则来进行环境选择。

Method: 采用设计科学研究方法论，结合量子软件工程文献以及组织和社会技术研究，构建了一个包含“重力井及其属性”和“社会技术期望”两个分析构念的评估框架，并通过示例案例进行演示和评估。

Result: 提出了一个社会技术评估框架，能够帮助从业者做出有意识、情境感知的环境选择，保持架构灵活性，支持领域的演进发展。

Conclusion: 该框架推进了量子生态系统理论的发展，并为组织和从业者在当前不断演变的量子计算领域提供了实用指导。

Abstract: Quantum computing environments are composed of heterogeneous layers spanning hardware, software development kits, and applications. Practitioners curating these environments face a fragmented and rapidly evolving landscape with few principled guides for navigation. This paper presents a framework for evaluating quantum computing environment choices through a socio-technical lens, developed using Design Science Research methodology. Drawing on the quantum software engineering literature as well as organizational and socio-technical research, the framework introduces three analytical constructs: gravity wells and their properties, which characterize how certain technologies and structural conditions exert increasing pull on surrounding environment choices, and socio-technical desiderata, which articulate the normative goals against which those pulls can be evaluated. The framework supports practitioners in making deliberate, context-aware environment choices that preserve architectural flexibility and support the evolutionary development of the field. Demonstration and evaluation of the framework is conducted through exemplary cases. The contribution advances both the theory of quantum ecosystems and the practical guidance available to organizations and practitioners navigating the current, evolving field of quantum computing.

### [179] [MM-IssueLoc: A Controlled Benchmark for Evaluating Visual Evidence in Multimodal Repository-Level Issue Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15205)
*Shaoxiong Zhan,Shi Hu,Boyu Feng,Hai Lin,Andrew Gong,Zhengda Zhou,Jiaying Zhou,Yunyun Hou,Hao Su,Hai-Tao Zheng*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出了MM-IssueLoc基准，用于评估仓库级问题定位中视觉证据的作用，包含652个实例和7类图像标注，实验表明现有系统在多模态问题定位上仍不可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的仓库级问题定位主要作为纯文本任务评估，而实际仓库问题常包含截图、错误对话框等视觉证据。已有的多模态SE基准将定位与补丁生成纠缠在一起，无法辨别视觉输入究竟有帮助、有害还是被忽略。

Method: 构建了包含652个issue-PR实例的MM-IssueLoc基准，覆盖23种语言，标注了7种图像类别和4个相关等级。提供文件级和函数级黄金标签，支持纯文本和带图像的成对评估，并设计了VCE诊断方法将图像转换为结构化文本证据。评估了基于LLM和检索的系统，包括MM-IssueLoc-VL-Emb多模态检索器。

Result: 最强agent达到38.96文件级Acc@5和22.45函数级Acc@10，最强检索器达到33.86函数级Acc@10。跨基准比较表明，在文本主导的SWE基准上的高定位分数不能干净地迁移到多模态问题定位。

Conclusion: MM-IssueLoc将视觉证据转化为明确的评估变量，使未来工作能够测试系统是否真正通过利用视觉证据来提高定位性能，而非依赖纯文本线索或下游补丁生成效应。

Abstract: Real repository issues routinely include visual evidence such as screenshots, error dialogs, rendered UI states, and logs, yet repository-level issue localization is evaluated mostly as a text-only task. Existing multimodal SE benchmarks evaluate end-to-end repair, entangling localization with patch synthesis and obscuring whether visual input helped, hurt, or was ignored. We introduce \textbf{MM-IssueLoc}, a controlled benchmark and evaluation protocol for repository-level localization with visual evidence. MM-IssueLoc contains 652 issue-PR instances across 23 languages, with annotations for 7 image categories and 4 relevance levels. It provides file-level and function-level gold labels, paired text-only and with-image evaluation, and VCE-based diagnostics that convert images into structured textual evidence. We evaluate LLM-based and retrieval-based systems, including MM-IssueLoc-VL-Emb as a controlled multimodal retriever. Results show that existing systems remain far from reliable multimodal repository localization: the strongest agent reaches 38.96 file Acc@5 and 22.45 function Acc@10, while the strongest retriever reaches 33.86 function Acc@10. Cross-benchmark comparisons show that high localization scores on text-dominant SWE benchmarks do not transfer cleanly to multimodal issue localization. MM-IssueLoc turns visual evidence into an explicit evaluation variable, enabling future work to test whether systems improve by using visual evidence for localization, rather than by relying on text-only cues or downstream patch-generation effects.

</details>

### [180] [Majority Correctness in Social Networks: From Well-Mixed Electorates to Complex Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14288)
*Dan Braha,Marcus A. M. de Aguiar*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究社交网络中投票前持续社会互动对多数正确性的影响，提出狂热-逆向选民模型，发现社会互动可能降低多数投票准确性，且仅当更新机制为纯粹从众时，无限选民下的多数优势才能保持；网络拓扑结构通过影响选民相关性调节多数准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于Condorcet陪审团定理，探讨当投票前存在社交网络上的持续互动时，多数投票能否选出客观正确选项，以及社会互动对集体决策准确性的影响。

Method: 提出狂热-逆向选民模型，结合模仿与对立两种更新机制；对完全混合群体进行解析分析，建立有限选民Condorcet型保证，并通过Erdős–Rényi、无标度、环和小世界网络进行仿真验证。

Result: 社会互动可能降低多数准确性；仅在纯粹从众时无限选民下的多数优势成立；任何持续逆向更新会使个体与多数正确性退化为随机水平；网络拓扑影响相关性：枢纽主导网络产生强正相关、低准确性，空间结构网络产生弱相关、高准确性。

Conclusion: 社会互动在集体决策中既可能带来有限选民层面的Condorcet优势，也可能导致聚合失败；网络拓扑结构是关键调节因素，纯从众是维持无限选民多数优势的关键条件。

Abstract: We study majority correctness when voting is preceded by sustained social interaction on a social network. Motivated by the Condorcet Jury Theorem, we consider a binary choice with an objectively correct alternative, where uninformed voters revise their vote intentions through repeated interaction in the presence of competing committed leaders (zealots). In this zealot--contrarian voter model, voters may either imitate or oppose the views they encounter. For fully mixed electorates, we characterize the long-run distribution of votes and the correlation structure induced among voters, and we show that Erdős--Rényi networks exhibit the same majority-correctness behavior after an appropriate rescaling of leader influence. Building on these results, we establish a finite-electorate Condorcet-type guarantee: when post-deliberation individual correctness exceeds random choice, a strict majority is more likely to select the correct alternative than a randomly chosen voter. At the same time, we identify an aggregation failure: social interaction can reduce majority accuracy relative to a no-deliberation benchmark in which voters respond only to zealots. As the electorate size tends to infinity, this finite-electorate advantage disappears unless social updating is purely conformist, revealing a tipping point at full conformity: any persistent contrarian updating drives both individual and majority correctness to the random choice level of one half. Simulations on scale-free, ring, and small-world networks further show that topology matters because it shapes the vote correlations generated by social influence: hub-dominated structures generate stronger positive correlations and lower majority accuracy, whereas spatially structured networks generate weaker correlations, preserve a larger effective number of independent judgments, and improve majority accuracy.

</details>


### [181] [Prices, Probabilities, and Parlays: Systematic Bias in Sports Prediction Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14430)
*Niusha Moshrefi*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文通过对Kalshi交易所2300万条体育赛事交易数据的研究，发现预测市场价格作为概率解读存在两个系统性偏差：1）校准偏差在合约到期前10分钟急剧恶化；2）跨游戏串关投注系统性地被高估。这些偏差源于交易者的保险需求和市场层面的定价加成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验预测市场价格是否可靠地反映真实概率，因为学术研究和衍生品市场都广泛依赖这种概率解读，但系统性偏差的存在会严重影响其实际应用价值。

Method: 利用Kalshi交易所2300万条主流体育联盟的moneyline交易数据，通过时间到期分桶的校准模型分析价格校准的动态变化，同时对比串关投注价格与单个合约价格的乘积，检验系统性的定价偏差。

Result: 1）校准参数在合约生命周期中期接近完美校准参考值，但在到期前10分钟急剧偏离，校准曲线呈现阶梯状，曲率参数远高于1（与经典彩票选择中的符号相反）；2）跨游戏串关投注系统性地高于各leg价格乘积，且随leg数量增加而增大，即便在单leg校准几乎完美的时段也如此。

Conclusion: 预测市场价格作为概率使用时不能仅依赖价格本身，必须考虑合约到期时间和产品类型因素。两种偏差都具有系统性，因此可以通过计算方法进行修正。

Abstract: Prediction market prices are routinely interpreted as probabilities, both in academic work and in derivative products built atop these markets. We document two systematic ways this interpretation fails on Kalshi, a major U.S. event-contract exchange, using 23 million moneyline trades across major sport leagues. First, calibration, the agreement between quoted prices and realized event frequencies, is not a static property of a contract: fitting calibration models within time-to-expiry buckets, we find that parameters sit at their perfect-calibration reference values in the middle of a contract's life but depart sharply as expiry approaches. In the final ten minutes before settlement the empirical calibration curve becomes step-like, fitting a Prelec form with curvature parameter well above one, the opposite sign of the canonical lottery-choice fit, consistent with insurance-demand behavior by traders holding losing positions. Second, cross-game parlays on Kalshi are systematically overpriced relative to the product of their contemporaneous leg prices, with overpricing growing in leg count. This holds when the parlay legs are drawn from the TTE regime in which leg-level calibration is essentially perfect, indicating a separate, market-level markup at the parlay-pricing stage. Both deviations are systematic and therefore admit computational correction. Practical use of prediction-market prices as probabilities requires conditioning on time to expiry and on product type, not on price alone.

</details>


### [182] [Manufactured Divisiveness: Decomposing the Hostile Content of Seven Social Media Influence Operations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14491)
*Emilio Ferrara*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 该研究分析了国家支持的影响力行动中的仇恨言论，发现现有检测工具将30.4%的党派攻击和19.5%的地缘政治谩骂错误归类为仇恨言论。实际真正的身份仇恨仅占约50.1%，而严重到含非人化或煽动的仇恨仅18.7%。七次行动可分为三类：身份仇恨（俄方）、地缘政治谩骂（伊朗）和党派分裂（委内瑞拉）。作者提出"制造的分裂"这一概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将国家支持的影响力行动中的内容普遍标记为"仇恨"或"毒性"，但这种测量存在误差——检测器被验证为捕捉更广泛的定义（包括针对外群体的敌意或分裂性），从而将党派或地缘政治谩骂错误归因于仇恨。作者希望区分真正的仇恨与其他形式的分裂性言论。

Method: 使用Twitter信息操作档案中7次政府归因行动的25.08M条推文（8,275个账户）。首先验证基于两个提示的LLM检测器（与人类标签一致度Cohen's κ=0.82）来识别广义敌意；然后开发可审计规则（与专家一致度κ=0.52）将5,457条帖子进一步分为三类。

Result: 约50.1%是身份攻击，30.4%是党派攻击，19.5%是针对国家及外交政策的谩骂。仅18.7%同时满足身份攻击且含非人化或煽动。七次行动分为三组：身份仇恨（俄方IRA和RU-op）、地缘政治谩骂（伊朗两次行动）和党派分裂（委内瑞拉两次行动）。

Conclusion: 将检测到的言论全部报告为仇恨会夸大约两倍的实际仇恨率。专家在最困难案例上仅中度一致（κ=0.37-0.50），最好的19个LLM模型κ=0.601。作者提出"制造的分裂"这一共享产物，并呼吁重新定义在线话语中仇恨的研究。

Abstract: State-backed influence operations are routinely measured as high-prevalence sources of ``hate'' and ``toxicity.'' We argue those rates rest on a measurement error: the detectors behind them are validated to catch a broader definition inclusive of hostility or divisiveness aimed at an out-group, and so over-attribute hate to content better described as partisan or geopolitical invective. Across 25.08M tweets from seven government-attributed campaigns in the Twitter Information Operations archive (8,275 accounts), we separate hate from the other forms of divisiveness. We first validate a two-prompt LLM-based detector, matching human labels at Cohen's $κ=0.82$, to identify the broader hostility; we then develop an auditable rule, agreeing with an expert at $κ=0.52$, to further classify this content (5,457 posts) into three sub-categories. About 50.1% are identity-based attacks on people, whereas 30.4% are partisan attacks and 19.5% invective against states and their foreign policy. Reporting all of it as hate therefore overstates hate roughly twofold; only 18.7% is both identity-based and dehumanizing or inciting. Six of seven campaigns sort into three regimes that a single ``hate'' rate flattens, namely identity hate (RU-op and IRA, both Russia-attributed), geopolitical invective (both Iran operations), and partisan divisiveness (both Venezuela operations). We call the shared product $manufactured divisiveness$. The line to separate these constructs itself remains unsettled: on the hardest cases three independent human experts agree only moderately (pairwise $κ=0.37$--$0.50$), and the best of nineteen LLM models tops out at $κ=0.601$ against the experts' majority. Our findings can help redefine the study of hate in the context of influence campaigns and broader online discourse.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重叠社区检测算法难以在检测质量和可扩展性之间取得良好平衡。

Method: 提出Highway算法，通过利用输入网络的稀疏骨干结构进行高效的社区推理。

Abstract: Community structures are common in real networks, and extracting them provides valuable insight in applications ranging from drug discovery to market segmentation. We, therefore, propose Highway, a scalable OCD algorithm that exploits the sparse backbone of the input network to perform efficient community inference. We used 728 Lancichinetti-Fortunato-Radicchi benchmark networks to compare Highway and its ablated version against 10 existing OCD algorithms. Our results, based on five performance measures, demonstrate a competitive performance for Highway. It ranks first in overlapping normalized mutual information with a 6.9% improvement over the strongest baseline. It also ranks second in all the other four performance measures. These comparative results suggest that Highway coupled with its backbone procedure offers a suitable accuracy-efficiency trade-off. The Highway algorithm is open-source and available as part of the CDlib library.

*Celina Treuillier,Sylvain Castagnos,Armelle Brun*

Conclusion: GRAIL不仅提供个体层面的极化度量，还通过创新评估框架实现了对识别行为的更精细刻画与解释。

We propose GRAIL, the first individual polarization metric, relying on multiple factors. GRAIL assesses these factors through entropy and is based on an adaptable Generalized Additive Model. We evaluate the proposed metric on a Twitter dataset related to the highly controversial debate about the COVID-19 vaccine. Experiments confirm the ability of GRAIL to discriminate between polarization behaviors. ### [185] [Intelligent Three Level Learning Architecture for Autonomous UAV Swarms in Search and Rescue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14093)
*Oleksii Bychkov*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种三层层次化学习架构用于自主无人机蜂群搜救，整合Hebbian神经可塑性、多智能体强化学习+图神经网络+行为树、MAML+BDI推理+数字孪生三种不同机制，通过22个架构契约提供6类形式化保证，引入蜂群元认知概念，并通过主集成定理证明混合神经符号系统可保持所有保证类别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在无人机蜂群搜救中通常对各个层次应用单一学习范式，无法充分利用不同层次（反射、技能、推理）的优势，存在层次间不一致、缺乏形式化保证等问题。

Method: 提出三层层次化学习架构：(1) 底层：Hebbian神经可塑性用于个体适应；(2) 中层：多智能体强化学习+GNN+行为树用于战术协调；(3) 顶层：MAML+BDI推理+数字孪生用于战略决策。通过22个架构契约（6组件）提供6类形式化保证（安全性、预算正确性、最优性、活性、无饥饿、层次间一致性），引入蜂群元认知作为组合属性。

Result: 主集成定理证明当所有契约满足时，混合神经符号系统可保持全部6类保证；动态情况下额外5个契约扩展框架，增加认知弹性、优雅降级和单调元改进3项保证；理论上解决现有层次化RL的五项基本局限性。

Conclusion: 该架构通过形式化契约和不同学习机制的有机整合，为无人机蜂群搜救提供了一种兼具形式化保证和灵活性的混合智能方案。

Abstract: This paper presents a novel three level hierarchical learning architecture for autonomous UAV swarms performing search and rescue operations. Unlike conventional approaches that apply a single learning paradigm across all hierarchy levels, the proposed architecture integrates three qualitatively different learning mechanisms corresponding to the biological hierarchy of reflexes, skills, and reasoning such as Hebbian neuroplasticity for individual agent adaptation, multi agent reinforcement learning with graph neural networks and behavior trees for tactical coordination, and model agnostic meta learning with BDI reasoning and a digital twin for strategic decision making.
  The architecture is formalized through twenty two architectural contracts organized across six components such as BDI, Behavior Trees, GNN, MARL, Neuroplasticity, Meta Learning that collectively provide six classes of formal guarantees such as safety, budget correctness, optimality, liveness, starvation freedom, and inter level consistency.
  We introduce Swarm Meta Cognition as a compositional property arising from the structured interaction of all three levels, enabling the swarm to monitor its own cognitive state and switch between cognitive strategies. Five constructive progress functions for SAR task types bridge the gap between abstract optimization theory and concrete operational scenarios.
  The main integration theorem establishes that when all contracts are satisfied, the hybrid neuro-symbolic system preserves all six guarantee classes. For the dynamic case with active learning, five new contracts extend the framework with three additional guarantees such as cognitive resilience, graceful degradation, and monotonic meta improvement. Theoretical analysis demonstrates that the architecture addresses five fundamental limitations of existing hierarchical RL approaches.

</details>


### [186] [HG-RAG: Hierarchy-Guided Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Structured Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14095)
*Pranav Yadav*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HG-RAG通过层次化知识图谱的图遍历检索，替代传统扁平文档检索，提升了LLM在层次、关系和多跳推理任务上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RAG系统仅从扁平文档库检索上下文，无法处理需要层次结构或关系推理的查询，导致在处理结构化知识时效果不佳。

Method: 提出HG-RAG框架：1) 从查询中识别命名实体锚点；2) 通过父节点向上扩展、关系邻居横向扩展、子节点向下扩展进行图遍历；3) 将层次化结构上下文输入LLM。

Result: 在三种规模（18-800节点）和四类查询（局部事实、层次、邻域、多跳）上，HG-RAG在层次、关系和多跳推理任务中持续优于密集检索基线，同时减少幻觉并保持局部一致性。

Conclusion: HG-RAG证明了层次化知识图谱引导的检索能有效弥补传统RAG在结构化推理上的不足，为需要复杂关系理解的场景提供了新方案。

Abstract: Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) has proven to be a widely successful process at improving the quality of outputs from a Large Language Model (LLM) for wider context. However, RAG systems typically retrieve context from flat document stores, which struggles when queries require hierarchical or relational reasoning across structured knowledge. I present HG-RAG (Hierarchy-Guided RAG), a framework that performs graph-traversal over a hierarchical knowledge graph to deliver structured context to a language model. My retrieval pipeline resolves a named entity anchor from the query, then expands context upward through parent nodes, laterally through relational neighbors, and downward through child nodes when needed. I evaluate HG-RAG against a dense retrieval baseline across three world scales (18-800 nodes) with four query types: local fact, hierarchical, neighborhood, and multi-hop. Results show HG-RAG consistently outperforms the flat baseline on hierarchical, relational, and multi-hop reasoning tasks, while reducing hallucination and maintaining locality coherence.

### [187] [IMEX Interaction-Based Model Explanation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14096)
*Emiliano Massi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为IMEX的可解释预测建模方法，通过静态相关力（PCS）和交互相关力（PCI）两个互补指标，识别对预测目标贡献最大的特征及其交互作用，并在合成数据集上与INVASE方法进行了实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑盒模型虽然预测准确，但缺乏透明性，难以解释其内部决策机制。在关键应用场景中，仅靠预测精度不足以验证模型有效性，亟需能够揭示预测背后原因的解释方法。

Method: IMEX框架包含两个核心指标：PCS（量化单个特征贡献）和PCI（捕捉特征间的非加性效应）。该方法不限制高阶交互分析，可探索大于2的特征子集交互模式，构建预测的可解释性图谱。

Result: 通过三个已知结构的合成数据集，将IMEX的PCS组件与INVASE方法进行对比实验。结果表明，在特征与预测目标之间存在非线性、条件性和多重共线性关系时，IMEX能够有效恢复相关特征级别的结构。

Conclusion: IMEX是一种有效的可解释预测建模方法，能够识别重要特征及其交互作用，在复杂数据关系下优于或可比于现有方法，为黑盒模型提供更透明的解释机制。

Abstract: In predictive modeling, the ability to explain why a model produces a given target prediction has become increasingly important [5, 10]. Black-box models do not provide a transparent description of the internal mechanisms that generate the prediction, making even accurate predictions difficult to interpret and validate. In critical contexts, predictive accuracy alone is not a sufficient validation metric if the reasons underlying model decisions remain unexplained. The IMEX (Interaction-Based Model Explanation) approach represents a methodological direction within explainable predictive modeling. IMEX is designed to identify which variables contribute most to the target prediction and which interactions among variables are significant in determining the target. The method does not impose limitations on higher-order interaction analysis, allowing the investigation of feature subsets with cardinality greater than two. Beyond the identification of feature importance, IMEX enables the exploration of interaction patterns that may be consistent with latent mechanisms influencing the outcome. Through the application of the IMEX algorithm, it is possible to construct an interpretability map of the predictions. The IMEX framework is built on two complementary metrics: Static Correlation Power (PCS), which quantifies the contribution of individual features, and Interaction Correlation Power (PCI), which captures non-additive effects among features. In the present work, the PCS component is experimentally validated through a comparison with INVASE [18] on three synthetic datasets with known structures. The results indicate that IMEX can recover relevant feature-level structures in the presence of non-linear, conditional, and multicollinear relationships between input features and prediction targets.

Candidates are ranked by evidence consistency across networks (Both, TCGA-only, GREmLN-only). The system is implemented as a multi-agent LangGraph DAG workflow, accessible through a unified Python API and Model Context Protocol (MCP) client, operating as a downstream analytical layer over precomputed regulatory networks rather than a network inference method. Across eleven breast cancer (BRCA) and twelve colorectal cancer (COAD) focal genes, RegNetAgents identifies candidate regulators significantly enriched for OncoKB-annotated cancer genes. ### [192] [Capability from Access Structure, Not Scale: Lower Bounds and Pre-Registered Tests for Hybrid Sequence Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14144)
*Wenhui Chen,Jianlin Chen,Ziyao Lin,Chi Man Vong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出能力收敛假说（CCH）：在固定推理预算下，表征收敛不意味着能力收敛；能力收敛于"存取完备混合体"——同时具备压缩O(1)状态通道和可扩展逐字索引通道的架构。基于牛顿苹果问题，识别出三条资源墙（Shannon墙、horizon墙、circuit墙），混合架构通过分别支付各墙代价跨越三者。预注册小规模实验验证了剪刀差效应等关键预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 柏拉图表征假说（PRH）认为模型规模扩大时异质网络的表征会收敛于共享现实模型，但表征收敛是否必然带来能力收敛？作者质疑这一隐含假设，提出能力收敛可能遵循截然不同的规律。

Method: 提出CCH假说，以牛顿苹果问题（无限流）为见证任务，识别三条信息论/计算复杂性下界（Shannon墙、horizon墙、circuit墙）；证明同时具备压缩状态通道和索引通道的混合架构可跨越所有三条墙；通过预注册实验验证剪刀差效应。

Result: 预注册实验显示：精确检索误差剪刀差（0.994 vs 0.000，64标量状态+全局注意力层）、状态跟踪分岔落在注册边界、合取见证显示不可约的双通道解决方案；一项预测失败（方向相反）并如实报告。

Conclusion: 表征收敛由规模免费提供；能力收敛必须通过存取结构购买。表征收敛不蕴含能力收敛，能力的收敛轨迹由架构的资源墙跨越能力决定。

Abstract: The Platonic Representation Hypothesis (PRH) holds that as models scale, representations of heterogeneous networks converge toward a shared model of reality. We propose its sequel and boundary, the Capability Convergence Hypothesis (CCH): under a fixed per-token inference budget, representational convergence does not entail capability convergence. Capability instead converges toward a class, the access-complete hybrid: any architecture holding both a compressive O(1)-state channel and a scalable verbatim-index channel. We anchor it on a witness task, the Newton's-apple problem in an infinite stream, and name three resource walls: a Shannon wall barring any o(Nb)-state architecture, a horizon wall barring any fixed window, and a circuit wall barring fixed-depth attention-only composition (conditional on TC0 != NC1). Under an explicit separability assumption a hybrid crosses all three by paying each wall's price, so capability is strictly super-additive under composition. We separate what we prove from what we conjecture: the access-completeness principle rests on information-theoretic lower bounds and pre-registered experiments, while the field-level convergence trend is an economics-motivated conjecture. We report the first pre-registered small-scale tests under criteria frozen before the data: the predicted scissors gap is measured (exact-retrieval error 0.994 vs. 0.000 once a 64-scalar state gains one global-attention layer), the state-tracking bifurcation lands at the registered boundary, and a conjunction witness shows an irreducibly two-channel solution; one prediction failed with its direction reversed and is reported as such. Representational convergence is given freely by scale; capability convergence must be purchased by access structure.

</details>

### [194] [ToolAnchor: Anchoring Counterfactual Context to Boost Agentic Tool-use Capability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14145)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出ToolAnchor框架：(1) 使用教师模型在关键决策点假设反事实锚点上下文；(2) 通过学生模型推演验证这些上下文；(3) 将成功的干预通过智能体后训练内化。通过注入反事实上下文打破行为惯性，恢复失败的轨迹。

Result: 在通用AI助手(GAIA)、文本搜索(BrowseComp)和视觉搜索(VDR-Bench)三类任务中，ToolAnchor在扩展工具集下展现出一致的竞争力表现。

Abstract: Tool-augmented large language model agents excel at long-horizon tasks, yet they are typically post-trained on fixed toolsets. When tasks demand new tools, these agents struggle to incorporate them effectively, and retraining from scratch is often impractical. We identify the core obstacle in such toolset expansion problem as behavioral inertia: the tendency of agents to fall back on familiar tools and established reasoning patterns despite having access to new ones. We demonstrate that injecting counterfactual anchor contexts at critical decision points can break this inertia, recovering failed trajectories by eliciting suppressed agent capabilities. To scale this insight, we propose ToolAnchor, a framework that uses teacher models to hypothesize these counterfactual contexts, verifies them via student rollouts, and internalizes the successful interventions through agentic post-training. Extensive evaluations across general AI assistant (GAIA), textual search (BrowseComp), and visual search (VDR-Bench) tasks demonstrate that ToolAnchor consistently exhibits competitive performance under expanded toolsets. Our work bridges the gap between static post-training and dynamic adaptation, charting a new path for scalable agentic reinforcement learning.

Motivation: 大语言模型零样本推理性能优异但部署成本高昂且不环保；小语言模型是可持续的替代方案，但在复杂多跳逻辑推理任务中容易出错。本文旨在通过神经符号代理框架提升小语言模型的推理能力。

Method: 将小语言模型转化为极简代理，配备两个专用工具调用：extract_facts（符号三元组提取）和 get_hint（通过关系图卷积网络 RGCN 进行专家推理）。在 Oracle 场景（真实三元组）和 Realistic 场景（自提取知识）两种配置下评估 Gemma 3 (1B, 4B) 和 Llama 3.2 (3B)。

Result: RGCN 提示相比仅基于故事的基线方法带来 1.5-2 倍性能提升；系统受限于提取瓶颈和顺序演绎脆弱性（早期提取误差在多跳链中累积）；在特定架构中发现了"干扰效应"——尽管有专家提示，自生成的噪声事实仍会降低性能。

Conclusion: 本文刻画了低资源代理系统中符号落地的挑战，并为神经符号代理流水线中的迭代验证提供了路线图。

Abstract: Although large language models (LLMs) have set benchmarks for zero-shot reasoning, their deployment remains cost-prohibitive and environmentally taxing. Small Language Models (SLMs) offer a sustainable alternative, but prone to errors, on tasks requiring complex, multi-hop logical grounding. We investigate a neuro-symbolic agentic framework to enhance the reasoning capabilities of SLMs, specifically Gemma 3 (1B, 4B) and Llama 3.2 (3B), using the CLUTRR kinship benchmark. Our approach transforms the SLM into a minimalist agent utilizing two specialized tool calls: extract_facts for symbolic triplet extraction and get_hint for expert reasoning via a Relational Graph Convolutional Network (RGCN). We evaluate these models across two configurations, both in an Oracle scenario with ground-truth triplets and a Realistic scenario relying on self-extracted knowledge. Our results reveal that while RGCN-derived hints provide a 1.5 - 2x performance gain over story-only baselines, the system is constrained by the extraction bottleneck and sequential deductive fragility, where early extraction errors compound over multi-hop chains. Furthermore, we identify a "distraction effect" in specific architectures where noisy, self-generated facts degrade performance despite the presence of expert hints. This work characterizes the challenges of symbolic grounding in low-resource agentic systems and provides a roadmap for iterative verification in neuro-symbolic agentic pipelines.

</details>

### [197] [MemoHarness: Agent Harnesses That Learn from Experience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14159)
*Yue Huang,Wenjie Wang,Han Bao,Yuchen Ma,Xiaonan Luo,Yi Nian,Haomin Zhuang,Zheyuan Liu,Yue Zhao,Xiangliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MemoHarness是一种自适应agent框架优化方法，将框架分解为六个可编辑的控制维度，通过双层经验库存储诊断信息和全局模式，并利用检索到的经验为每个测试案例自适应调整框架，无需测试时标签、反馈或额外搜索，在多个基准测试中优于固定框架，且具有选择性的跨场景迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有agent大多使用单一全局框架（harness），而框架设计对agent行为影响显著，但大多数自动优化方法只优化提示词、管道或工作流等较窄的工件的，忽视了框架本身的适应性优化。

Method: 将agent框架分解为上下文管理、工具调用、编排、记忆、解码和输出处理六个可编辑维度；构建双层经验库（per-case诊断+全局模式）；通过检索经验为每个测试案例自适应调整框架，无需测试时标签或反馈。

Result: 在shell-agent、代码生成和分析推理三个基准测试中，MemoHarness优于固定框架基线；展现出选择性的跨数据集和跨基座模型迁移能力；当检索经验可缓存时，额外上下文开销具有成本竞争力。

Conclusion: 执行经验是构建比单一静态配置更具适应性的agent框架的实用基础，但关于统计稳健性和组件归因的更广泛声明留待未来工作。

Abstract: An agent harness is the external control layer that turns a base LLM into an executable agent by managing context, tools, orchestration, memory, decoding, and output handling. While harness design strongly affects agent behavior, most automatic improvement methods optimize narrower artifacts such as prompts, pipelines, or workflows, and deployed agents usually reuse a single global harness for all cases. We introduce MemoHarness, an adaptive harness optimization framework that learns from its own executions. MemoHarness decomposes the harness into six editable control dimensions, stores per-case diagnoses and distilled global patterns in a dual-layer experience bank, and adapts the learned harness to each test case using retrieved experience without test-time labels, feedback, or additional search. In our evaluation across shell-agent, code-generation, and analytical-reasoning benchmarks, MemoHarness improves over the fixed harnesses we compare against and shows selective transfer to unseen suites and base models. Its additional context can also remain cost-competitive when much of the retrieved experience is cacheable. These results provide evidence that execution experience is a practical substrate for building agent harnesses that are more adaptive than a single static configuration, while leaving broader claims about statistical robustness and component attribution to future work.

### [198] [When a Verified World Model Still Loses: Play-Adequacy vs Prediction-Accuracy in LLM-Synthesized Code World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14169)
*Javier Aguilar Martín*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文指出，用LLM合成可执行代码形式的“世界模型”（CWM）来辅助规划时，通常以采样轨迹上的高过渡准确率来判断模型是否合格。作者证明这是一种错误的标准：一个在采样上100%准确、在规划搜索分布上≥98%状态准确的CWM，仍会因<1%的关键错误而在游戏中系统性失败。作者称此为“验证与正确性差距”，并给出了量化的危险公式，证明该问题无法通过增加数据修复，且同样适用于不完全信息博弈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流做法用采样轨迹上的过渡准确率来验证LLM合成的世界模型，但作者认为这对规划而言是错误的充分性标准——因为模型在罕见但关键的状态转移上犯错，足以导致规划失败。

Method: 作者通过端到端实验展示了LLM合成CWM的“验证与正确性差距”，提出量化公式 danger = play_cost × (1 - rarity)^N，证明遗漏规则造成的危害遵循该定律；并证明LLM合成是规则翻译而非规则推理，增加数据（DAgger、针对性示例）无法修复；对不完全信息博弈，给出覆盖界 N ≳ b^{d_max}，并构造了Beacon反例。

Result: 一个通过采样100%准确、搜索分布上≥98%状态准确的CWM，仍因<1%的关键错误在游戏中系统性失败（遗漏规则的游戏代价为0.091）；该危害遵循量化定律；LLM无法通过更多数据推断遗漏规则；不完全信息博弈中也存在同样机制。

Conclusion: 面向规划的世界模型是否充分，不应以采样过渡的预测准确率衡量，而应在搜索分布上评估或直接通过游戏表现验证。

Abstract: Large language models can synthesize a game's rules as executable code - a Code World Model (CWM) - which a classical planner then searches over. Such models are typically accepted when they reach high transition accuracy on sampled trajectories. We argue this is the wrong notion of adequacy for planning.
  We show four things. (1) An LLM-synthesized CWM can pass a sampling gate at 100% transition accuracy and be $\geq 98\%$ state-accurate on the planner's own search distribution, yet lose systematically at play, because the $<1\%$ it gets wrong is exactly the pivotal dynamics; the play cost of the omitted rule is $0.091$ (seed-clustered 95% CI $[0.065,0.117]$, $n=4800$). We call this the verified-vs-correct gap, and confirm it end-to-end through the synthesis pipeline. (2) The harm follows a quantitative law, $\mathrm{danger}=\mathrm{play\_cost}\times(1-\mathrm{rarity})^N$, whose $(1-\mathrm{rarity})^N$ gate-miss factor is proven exact and whose play cost is empirically bounded. (3) The failure is not repaired by more data: LLM synthesis behaves as rule translation, not rule inference, and did not infer the omitted rule across models (GPT-5.x) and data regimes (including DAgger and targeted examples). (4) The same mechanism recurs on the belief-inference function of imperfect-information CWMs: we prove a coverage bound (a size-$N$ gate is identifying when $N\gtrsim b^{d_{\max}}$), explaining why shallow games such as Kuhn poker show no gap, and hand-construct Beacon, a verified-but-wrong inference function that passes the gate yet loses every game.
  These results suggest adequacy for planning-oriented world models should be measured on the search distribution or by play directly, not by prediction accuracy on sampled transitions.

</details>


### [199] [ReasFlow: Assisting Reasoning-Centric Scientific Discovery in Applied Mathematics via a Knowledge-Based Multi-Agent System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14178)
*Yutong He,Daibo Li,Guohong Li,Jiahe Geng,Zhengyang Huang,Can Ren,Zekun Zhang,Yifan Liu,Shuchen Zhu,Hengrui Zhang,Boao Kong,Ming Sun,Shu Li,Chenyi Li,Jiang Hu,Kun Yuan,Zaiwen Wen,Pingwen Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ReasFlow 是一个端到端自主智能体系统，用于以推理为中心的科学发现。它采用人类专家（首席研究员）与AI智能体（研究生）协作的范式，通过内部验证循环、知识检索与自我改进机制，实现从文献综述、算法设计、定理证明到论文撰写的全流程自动化。在生成五篇完整研究论文的测试中，ReasFlow 在LLM评审标准下取得了优于现有开源基线的成绩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化科研系统主要聚焦于经验驱动领域（有定量基准），而在需要严格证明和领域知识综合的理论驱动发现（尤其是数学基础学科）方面探索不足。主要挑战包括：理论推理的大规模验证困难、自主前沿探索的推理能力不足、以及文献中程序性启发知识的匮乏。

Method: ReasFlow 采用"人类PI + AI研究生"协作范式，核心包含两个机制：(i) 内部验证循环——在人类审查前审计逻辑一致性并纠正基础错误；(ii) 自动知识检索与自我改进机制——主动获取陈述性事实和被忽略的程序性启发知识。系统统一了文献综合、算法设计、定理证明、实验和论文撰写。

Result: 在最少提示词下自主生成五篇包含严格理论和实验内容的完整研究论文，在基于LLM的评审标准下，ReasFlow 在所有开源基线中获得了最高的评估分数。

Conclusion: ReasFlow 有效填补了理论驱动科学发现中自动化系统的空白，证明了协作式人机交互范式在数学推理密集型研究中的可行性。系统已通过 ReasLab 平台公开提供。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models have fueled autonomous AI agents capable of tackling complex scientific tasks, yet existing automated research systems remain predominantly focused on empirically driven domains with quantitative benchmarks, leaving theory-driven discovery, particularly in mathematically grounded disciplines requiring rigorous proofs and synthesis of domain knowledge, largely underexplored. Key challenges include the difficulty of verifying theoretical reasoning at scale, insufficient reasoning ability for autonomous frontier exploration, and a scarcity of procedural heuristics in the literature. We introduce ReasFlow, an end-to-end autonomous agent system for reasoning-centric scientific discovery that operationalizes a collaborative paradigm where the human expert acts as Principal Investigator while the agent executes rigorous derivations as a capable graduate student. ReasFlow incorporates (i) a robust internal verification loop that audits logical coherence and corrects fundamental errors prior to human inspection, and (ii) an automated knowledge retrieval and self-improvement mechanism that proactively surfaces both declarative facts and overlooked procedural heuristics, substantially reducing expert intervention. The system unifies literature synthesis, algorithm design, theorem proving, experimentation, and manuscript preparation in a single system. Deployed to autonomously generate five complete research papers with rigorous theoretical and empirical content from minimal prompts, ReasFlow consistently achieves the highest evaluation scores among state-of-the-art open-access baselines under a curated LLM-based review rubric. ReasFlow is publicly accessible via the ReasLab platform, providing a collaborative workspace for AI-assisted theoretical research. Github repo: https://github.com/ReasLab/ReasFlow.git.

### [200] [RxBrain: Embodied Cognition Foundation Model with Joint Language-Visual Reasoning and Imagination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14187)
*Haotian Liang,Mingkang Chen,Yufei Huang,Yuchun Guo,Xiaomeng Zhu,Xiangli Shi,Kaixuan Wang,Yunxuan Mao,Weijie Zhou,Ling Chen,Shirong Zeng,Yueyu Long,Yuchen Si,Yajuan Zhu,Xingyu Zhou,Minghui Wang,Wanjia He,Xin Yang,Lingzhu Xiang,Zhiqing Liu,Bohan Ma,Xiran Huang,Tianshuo Yang,Zhiheng Liu,Xuantang Xiong,Zisheng Lu,Ping Luo,Yao Mu,Han Hu,Zhengyou Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Hy-Embodied-RxBrain，一种联合语言-视觉推理与想象的具身认知基础模型。该模型通过统一的多模态Mixture-of-Transformers架构，将具身规划表示为语言抽象结构（任务分解、决策逻辑）与视觉想象（世界状态预测、子目标规划）互补的单一规划序列，并构建了自动管道将具身视频转化为文本-视觉联合规划监督。实验表明模型在具身理解与生成、连续机器人动作生成上表现良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有具身认知模型存在两大局限：视觉-语言模型侧重场景理解与文本决策，生成式世界模型主要预测未来视觉状态，二者均未能将高层任务推理与物理状态有效连接。因此，需要一种能联合语言推理与视觉想象的具身认知基础模型，实现规划步骤与物理状态的深度融合。

Method: 1) 提出统一的多模态Mixture-of-Transformers架构，在一个模型中同时支持语言、图像、视频的理解与生成；2) 将具身规划表示为单一规划序列，语言提供抽象结构（任务分解、规划原语、约束、时序、决策逻辑），视觉想象负责世界状态预测与子目标规划，将每一步规划与中间/最终物理状态关联；3) 构建自动管道，将具身视频分解为规划步骤并与视觉状态转换对齐，生成文本-视觉联合规划监督数据；4) 提出RxBrain-Bench评估基准。

Result: 1) RxBrain在具身理解与生成任务上表现良好；2) 生成的规划具有耦合的文本推理、世界状态预测和联合子目标规划能力；3) 在连续机器人动作生成上，无需大规模动作数据预训练即可展现有前景的真实机器人性能。

Conclusion: RxBrain为具身认知基础模型迈出了初步一步，证明了语言抽象推理与视觉想象互补结合的有效性，有望弥合高层任务规划与物理执行之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: Embodied cognition requires agents to connect high-level task reasoning with the physical states to be achieved. We introduce Hy-Embodied-RxBrain, an embodied cognition foundation model with joint language-visual reasoning and imagination. Unlike vision-language models that emphasize scene understanding and textual decision making, or generative world models that mainly predict future visual states, RxBrain represents embodied plans in a single planning sequence where language and visual imagination play complementary roles. Language provides the abstract structure of a plan, including task decomposition, planning primitives, constraints, temporal order, and decision logic, while visual imagination grounds this structure through world state prediction and joint subgoal planning, associating each planning step with intermediate and final physical states. RxBrain adopts a unified multimodal Mixture-of-Transformers architecture that supports language, image, and video understanding and generation within one model. To train this capability, we build an automatic pipeline that converts embodied videos into joint text-visual planning supervision by decomposing videos into planning steps and aligning them with visual state transitions. We further introduce RxBrain-Bench to evaluate whether models can represent embodied plans through joint textual and visual components rather than separate understanding or generation. Experiments show that RxBrain maintains embodied understanding and generation abilities, and produces plans with coupled textual reasoning, world state prediction, and joint subgoal planning. We also extend RxBrain to continuous robot action generation, where it shows promising real-robot performance without large-scale action-data pretraining. These results provide an initial step toward foundation models for embodied cognition.

### [201] [How Artificial Intelligence LLM Engines Shape the Global Conflict Information Environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14197)
*Jason Miklian*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究发现，AI问答引擎在回答关于信息记录薄弱的冲突问题时更容易产生幻觉，且这种薄弱记录易被生成式引擎优化（GEO）操纵，存在虚假信息风险；通过对1,048个来源网站的分析，证实GEO源优化已在进行中，国家派系数字渗透虽初期但增长迅速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究AI问答引擎在回答和平与冲突相关问题时是否存在系统性的错误模式，以及这些错误反映了全球冲突信息环境的哪些变化。

Method: 对5个领先AI问答引擎就28个冲突问题进行测试，评分5,460个回答；分析1,048个AI引擎引用的冲突事实来源网站。

Result: 冲突的可检索记录越薄弱，引擎的虚构、错误归因和错误计数越严重；薄弱记录容易通过GEO被扭曲，且GEO源优化已在发生；国家派系数字渗透虽初现但增长迅速。

Conclusion: 呼吁回归深度本地监测和基于翻译的研究（AI无法替代的方法），以应对GEO信息战带来的挑战，并讨论未来研究机遇。

Abstract: Artificial Intelligence (AI) answer engines now field a growing share of the questions that analysts, scholars, and the public ask about issues of peace and conflict. Large Language Models (LLMs) are known to hallucinate under certain conditions, but do these errors have discernible patterns when they are asked about conflicts, and if so what can that teach us about the changing global conflict information environment? To answer, we first asked a battery of questions about 28 conflicts to five leading answer engines and scored their 5,460 answers against documented evidence. We found that the thinner the retrievable record around a given conflict, the more the engines invent, misattribute, and miscount. Thin records don't just encourage hallucination, but create structural exposure to mis- and disinformation, because they are the easiest records to warp through Generative Engine Optimization (GEO) to bias engine responses. Through an analysis of 1,048 websites that the AI LLMs pulled conflict facts from, we found that GEO source optimization is already happening, and while state-partisan digital capture remains incipient it is rapidly growing. We explain what these findings mean for scholarship with the rise of GEO information warfare, and for policy argue for a return to the deep local monitoring and translation-based research that AI tools cannot replicate, closing with a discussion of future research opportunities and challenges in this fast-moving space.
