### [259] [Can We Trust Item Response Theory for AI Evaluation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15190)
*Han Jiang,Sunbeom Kwon,Jinwen Luo,Ziang Xiao,Susu Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了将项目反应理论（IRT）应用于AI基准测试时，因数据分布与人类测试场景不匹配（模型少、题目多、能力分布偏态/多峰）所导致的估计可靠性问题。通过六个大语言模型基准的模拟实验，评估了四种估计工具在18,000种条件下的表现，发现经典估计器在大规模场景下不可行，而可扩展估计器在小样本或非正态分布下会产生不可靠的推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI基准测试越来越多地使用IRT等统计模型来评估模型能力、排序系统、选择信息样本和诊断基准质量。然而，AI基准数据（如模型数量少、题目数量多、能力分布偏态或多峰）与IRT最初应用于人类测试的数据特征存在显著差异。这种"数据体制不匹配"可能导致IRT估计的可靠性问题，需要系统评估。

Method: 从六个广泛使用的LLM基准中提取项目参数和能力分布，在三种常见IRT模型下模拟响应矩阵，然后比较四种估计工具：边际最大似然估计（MML）、马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）、变分推断（VI）和神经伪孪生估计器（neural pseudo-Siamese estimator）。在18,000种模拟条件下系统评估计算可行性、可扩展性以及关于模型排名、预测性能和项目特征的IRT推断的可靠性。

Result: 经典估计器（如MML、MCMC）在大型基准场景下变得不可行；可扩展估计器（如VI、神经估计器）在模型集较小或能力分布非正态时，会产生不可靠的项目级和排名推断。研究明确了在何种样本量和诊断条件下，潜特质模型能够可靠支持AI基准评估，以及何种情况下可能扭曲评估结论。

Conclusion: 将IRT应用于AI基准测试需要谨慎对待数据体制不匹配问题。需要足够的样本量和适当的诊断措施来确保可信使用，否则可能产生误导性的基准评估结论。

Abstract: AI benchmarks increasingly leverage item-level statistical models, particularly item response theory (IRT), to estimate model capabilities, rank systems, select informative examples, and diagnose benchmark quality. However, AI benchmark data often departs from the data regime of human testing, for which standard IRT estimation tools were originally developed: benchmarks typically involve fewer evaluated models, far more items, and capability distributions that may be skewed, clustered, or multimodal. We examine how these regime mismatches challenge the reliability of IRT modeling for AI evaluation. Using item parameters and capability distributions derived from six widely used LLM benchmarks, we simulate response matrices under three common IRT models and compare four estimation tools used in recent benchmark studies: marginal maximum likelihood, Markov chain Monte Carlo, variational inference, and a neural pseudo-Siamese estimator. Across 18,000 simulation conditions, we systematically evaluate computational feasibility, scalability, and the reliability of IRT inferences about model rankings, predicted performance, and item characteristics. Results show that classical estimators can become infeasible in large benchmark settings, whereas scalable estimators can produce unreliable item-level and ranking inferences with small or nonnormally distributed model sets. This study identifies when latent trait models reliably support or risk distorting AI benchmarking claims, and what sample sizes and diagnostics are needed for trustworthy use.

</details>


### [260] [Plover: Steering GUI Agents through Plan-Centric Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15193)
*Madhumitha Venkatesan,Shicheng Wen,Jiajing Guo,Jorge Piazentin Ono,Liu Ren,Dongyu Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉GUI代理的规划和适应过程是内部化的，用户无法检查、监督或纠正系统行为，导致在动态环境中难以控制代理的执行方向。

Method: 提出Plover系统，采用规划器-执行器架构，将任务计划和重新规划外部化为持久、可检查、可修改的工件，支持显式监督、局部修正编辑、自然语言引导和截图干预，同时在修复过程中保留已有进展。

Conclusion: 将计划和重新规划外部化为可见、可编辑的工件能显著提升GUI自动化系统的可修复性和用户控制力，是提升代理透明度和适应性的有效方向。

Abstract: Graphical user interface (GUI) automation remains challenging in real-world environments, where dynamic layouts, unexpected dialogs, and evolving interface states can cause autonomous agents to drift from user intent. Recent vision-based multimodal agents improve flexibility by operating directly over screenshots and natural language instructions, but planning and adaptation often remain internal, limiting users' ability to inspect, supervise, or correct system behavior. We present Plover, a plan-centric vision-based GUI automation system that externalizes task plans and replanning as persistent, inspectable, and revisable artifacts. Through a planner--executor architecture, Plover supports explicit supervision of evolving execution, localized correction through editable plans, natural-language guidance, and screenshot-grounded interventions, while preserving prior progress during repair. A formative study with six participants informed the interaction design. We then evaluate Plover through benchmark failure-case repair and scenario-based workflow analyses. Our results show that many autonomous GUI-agent failures are structurally repairable when plans remain visible and interventions are localized, and that explicit replanning helps make GUI automation more transparent, controllable, and adaptable.

### [261] [Self-Evolving Human-Centered Framework for Explainable Depression Symptom Annotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15202)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 抑郁症数据集的标签通常缺乏结构化证据、症状级理由以及与DSM-5-TR标准的可追溯对齐，限制了透明度和模型可解释性，标注质量成为心理健康领域XAI系统的主要瓶颈。

Method: 采用专家参与的三阶段框架：(1)候选证据选择，(2)DSM-5-TR标准级分析，(3)案例级综合生成标签。引入双记忆架构（示例记忆+反思记忆）内化专家反馈，无需重训即可迭代改进。

Result: 初步研究表明，该方法在专家评审样本上提高了标注一致性和可解释性，同时减少了人工修订工作量。

Abstract: Annotation quality is a major bottleneck in building reliable and explainable artificial intelligence (XAI) systems for mental health research. In depression-related datasets, labels are often assigned without structured evidence, symptom-level justification, or traceable alignment with the criteria of the Diagnostic and Statistical Manual of Mental Disorders, Fifth Edition, Text Revision (DSM-5-TR), limiting both transparency and downstream model interpretability. We propose a self-evolving, expert-in-the-loop annotation framework for Major Depressive Disorder (MDD) that combines large language model (LLM)-assisted labeling with expert verification. The framework is intended to support the construction of explainable, DSM-5-TR-aligned datasets rather than to perform clinical diagnosis. It operates in three stages: candidate evidence selection from textual records, criterion-level DSM-5-TR analysis, and case-level synthesis that produces label-level diagnostic and severity annotations. A dual-memory architecture, composed of Example Memory and Reflection Memory, is designed to internalize expert feedback and iteratively improve future annotations without retraining. We describe this mechanism and leave its evaluation across multiple feedback cycles to future work. In addition to final labels, the framework exports clinical evidence, reasoning traces, and edit histories, enabling comprehensive auditability. In a pilot study using expert-reviewed samples, the proposed approach improves annotation consistency and explainability while reducing manual revision effort.

</details>


### [262] [When Words Are Safe But Actions Kill: Probing Physical Danger Beyond Text Safety in Hidden-State Risk Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15218)
*Weimeng Wang,Ziqiang Wang,Zihang Zhan,Chuanpu Fu,Qi Li,Ke Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现大语言模型中内容危险（CD）与物理世界危险（PD）在表征层面可分离，提出基于隐状态探测的PRISM方法，在多个基准上实现高准确率（86-99%）和低误报率（0.7-13.7%），并构建了无显式危险词的物理安全对比基准PSB-1K。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全机制主要检测文本层面的有害内容，但LLM作为具身智能体的规划器时，一些语言上安全的指令在物理世界中执行可能造成真实危险。作者想探究这类物理危险（PD）是否与传统的内容危险（CD）是同一安全问题，以及能否在表征层面进行区分与检测。

Method: 1) 通过隐状态方向分析和随机分割零假设检验，证明CD与PD在LLM表征中是可分离信号；2) 提出PRISM——在全隐状态上训练的单层L2正则化逻辑回归探测头；3) 构建PhysicalSafetyBench-1K（PSB-1K），包含1000对物理风险样本，且不含直接危险关键词。

Result: PRISM在SafeAgentBench上达到86.2-87.7%准确率、11.7-13.7%误报率，而同规模LLM判决器误报率达24.7-39.0%；在PSB-1K上PRISM达99.6%准确率、0.7%误报率，对比Qwen2.5-3B判决器误拒67.8%安全任务；在SafeText和EARBench上也实现了可迁移的优异表现。

Conclusion: 物理危险与内容危险在表征层面本质不同且可分离；隐状态探测是一种有效的表征级物理安全方法，优于传统文本级别的安全审查；该方法具有良好的跨模型和跨任务泛化能力。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly serve as high-level planners for embodied agents, where linguistically benign instructions can become unsafe once grounded in the physical world. We study whether this physically grounded danger is the same safety problem as ordinary text-level content danger. Through hidden-state direction analysis and random-split null tests, we show that content danger (CD) and physical danger (PD) form separable signals in LLM representations across Qwen2.5-3B/7B/14B/32B, Phi-3.5 and SmolLM2. Building on the CD/PD separability, we propose PRISM, a single-layer L2-regularized logistic probe over full hidden states. PRISM achieves 86.2--87.7\% accuracy on SafeAgentBench with 11.7--13.7\% FPR, while same-scale LLM judges over-block safe tasks at 24.7--39.0\% FPR. We further introduce PhysicalSafetyBench-1K (PSB-1K), a contrastive benchmark of 1{,}000 physical-risk pairs without direct harm keywords, to test whether methods detect physically grounded danger rather than explicit unsafe wording. On PSB-1K, PRISM reaches 99.6\% accuracy and 0.7\% FPR, whereas a Qwen2.5-3B judge rejects 67.8\% of safe tasks. PRISM also replicates on SafeText and EARBench, supporting hidden-state probing as a representation-level method for physical safety beyond text moderation.

</details>

AutoSynthesis further supports heterogeneity analysis to examine how effect sizes vary across moderators, as well as risk-of-bias assessment. As output, AutoSynthesis produces a transparent report aligned with PRISMA guidelines. In our application, AutoSynthesis screened over 28 studies and extracted more than 20 quantitative claims. The pooled effect estimates produced by AutoSynthesis are similar to Hedges' $g$ of expert-conducted meta-analyses, indicating close agreement with manual evidence synthesis. We present teLLMe, a system for exploratory causal analysis of urban driving datasets. The system starts from a structured event table built from dashcam annotations and combines causal structure learning with the PC algorithm, bootstrap-based stability checks, and query-specific effect estimation using linear regression and DoWhy. Natural-language questions are mapped to structured causal queries through a schema-aware LLM, enabling users to specify treatments, outcomes, and subpopulations. teLLMe returns a "Causal Card" that summarizes effect estimates, adjustment sets, DAG support, and assumptions, followed by a short natural-language explanation. Case studies on BDD-derived traffic events show that the system can surface plausible relationships involving weather, peak hours, and traffic density, while making uncertainty and modeling choices explicit. The system is designed as a tool for hypothesis generation and expert reasoning rather than a source of definitive causal claims.

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SearchOS是一个多智能体框架，通过将隐式搜索状态外化为显式、持久化的共享状态（包括Frontier Task、证据图、覆盖图和失败记忆），并采用流水线并行调度和搜索工具中间件，来解决大语言模型在长交互中陷入重复搜索循环的问题，在WideSearch和GISA基准上取得领先结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具集成型大语言模型在长交互历史中难以跟踪任务进展，搜索失败时容易陷入重复循环，浪费搜索预算并影响最终输出质量。单智能体和多智能体系统均缺乏对搜索进度的显式管理。

Method: 1) 将开放域信息检索形式化为关系型模式补全（含引证）；2) 提出面向搜索的上下文管理（SOCM），将演化状态外化为Frontier Task、证据图、覆盖图和失败记忆；3) 流水线并行调度机制；4) 搜索工具中间件（拦截模型-工具交互、记录证据、处理停滞/预算耗尽）；5) 可复用的分层技能系统（策略技能+访问技能）。

Result: 在WideSearch和GISA基准上，SearchOS在所有评估指标上领先于单智能体和多智能体基线方法。

Abstract: Recent advances in Tool-Integrated Large Language Models have made web search a core capability of information-seeking agents. However, as interaction histories grow, agents increasingly struggle to track task progress. When search attempts fail to yield useful evidence, current single- and multi-agent systems can become trapped in repetitive loops, wasting search budgets and ultimately compromising the quality and completeness of the final output. We introduce SearchOS, a system-level multi-agent framework that turns fragile, implicit search progress into explicit, persistent, and shared state. First, we formulate open-domain information seeking as relational schema completion with grounded citations, where agents discover entities, populate attributes across linked tables, and anchor each value to source evidence. Then we design Search-Oriented Context Management (SOCM), which externalizes the evolving state into Frontier Task, an Evidence Graph, a Coverage Map, and Failure Memory. Built on SOCM, SearchOS applies a pipeline-parallel scheduling mechanism that overlaps the execution of sub-agents and continuously refills freed slots with tasks targeting unresolved coverage gaps to improve utilization and throughput. To schedule and control the execution of search agents, SearchOS introduces a Search Tool Middleware Harness that intercepts model and tool interactions to record grounded evidence and react to stalls or budget exhaustion, and provides a reusable hierarchical skill system comprising strategy and access skills to augment the agents' search process and avoid repeating failed search patterns across runs. On WideSearch and GISA, SearchOS leads all metrics among the evaluated single- and multi-agent baselines, paving the way toward robust information-seeking collaboration.

### [267] [Transition-Aware Routing in Hybrid Hollow-Core/Single-Mode Fiber Networks: A Cost--Throughput Investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14324)
*Md Ghulam Saber,Zhiping Jiang*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文研究混合空芯光纤（HCF）与单模光纤（SMF）网络中的路由权衡问题，提出多种保护路由方案，发现有限绕行的过渡感知路由（BD-TPAR）以仅1%的流量代价减少11%的过渡次数，是实际部署中的最佳选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在混合HCF/SMF网络中，HCF的增量部署会引入光纤类型转换（HCF-SMF过渡）带来的物理层性能惩罚。研究旨在探索如何在减少过渡次数与避免过度绕行之间取得平衡，并评估不同路由方案的效果。

Method: 使用事件驱动模拟器，比较六种保护路由方案（包括光纤盲、GSNR感知和显式过渡感知设计），在六种参考拓扑、五种HCF部署比例和300 Erlang动态负载下进行评估。模型包含每次过渡的GSNR惩罚和拼接故障可用性项。

Result: 最强过渡最小化方案（TPAR和GFJ）以20-25%的流量代价将过渡次数减半；GMR-T以3%的吞吐量代价减少22%的过渡；BD-TPAR以仅1%的代价减少11%的过渡。连续HCF部署可降低约40%的过渡次数并提升流量。

Conclusion: BD-TPAR是碎片化部署下的实际默认方案，GMR-T是低复杂度替代方案，TPAR或GFJ仅适用于过渡外部成本高的场景。

Abstract: Incremental deployment of hollow-core fiber (HCF) in single-mode-fiber (SMF) networks introduces a routing tradeoff: reducing HCF-SMF transitions can improve
  physical-layer feasibility, but overly transition-averse routing incurs harmful path detours. We study this tradeoff using a common event-driven simulator
  that compares six protected routing schemes spanning fiber-blind, generalized signal-to-noise ratio (GSNR)-aware, and explicitly transition-aware designs on
  hybrid HCF/SMF topologies. The model includes a per-transition GSNR penalty and an exploratory splice-failure availability term. Across six reference
  topologies, five HCF deployment fractions, and dynamic loads at 300 Erlang, the strongest transition minimizers, transition-penalty-aware routing (TPAR) and
  the GSNR/fiber-transition joint scheme (GFJ), halve the mean transition count at a 20-25% carried-traffic penalty. Among the intermediate designs, GSNR-
  maximal routing with transition-aware reranking (GMR-T) cuts transitions by approximately 22% relative to distance-adaptive routing and spectrum assignment
  (DA-RSA) at a 3% throughput cost, while bounded-detour TPAR (BD-TPAR) cuts transitions by approximately 11% at only a 1% cost. Deployment pattern also
  matters: contiguous HCF rollout lowers transitions by approximately 40% on average while improving carried traffic, reducing the benefit of aggressive
  transition-aware routing. These results support BD-TPAR as a practical default under fragmented deployment, GMR-T as a lower-complexity alternative, and TPAR
  or GFJ only where the external cost of transitions is high.

</details>

These flows are typically communicated via commodity network routers with conventional First-In-First-Out (FIFO) buffers. FIFO has proven to be the culprit of the well-known bufferbloat phenomenon, and the deployment of Active Queue Management (AQM) schemes have demonstrated significant performance improvements for latency-sensitive applications over the Internet in the IT domain. However, the bufferbloat phenomenon and the efficacy of AQM schemes have not been studied in IIoT-based OT domain. In this paper, we propose the use of AQM as a lightweight and non-intrusive mechanism for assisting mission-critical traffic flows in IIoT networks. ### [269] [Scheduler-Agnostic Adaptive-FEC for MPQUIC: Field Evaluation over Commercial Cellular Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14482)
*Takuma Tsubaki,Soto Anno,Seiya Komatsu,Takashi Torii,Takuya Tojo*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对MPQUIC Datagram的自适应FEC方案，通过复用QUIC丢包检测信号和现成的Reed-Solomon编码库，在车载蜂窝网络环境下显著降低了延迟和丢包率，且无需修改传输栈或调度器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MPQUIC Datagram虽能实现低延迟传输，但在车载蜂窝环境（如切换、无线条件剧烈变化）下对丢包非常脆弱。现有自适应FEC和编码多路径方案因需大幅修改传输栈或调度器，实际部署困难。

Method: 发送端利用QUIC丢包检测信号估计平滑后的每条路径丢包率，根据预期丢包自适应确定每个FEC块的校验包数量，复用现成的Reed-Solomon编码库，且无需改动调度器。

Result: 在三条商用LTE/5G链路的车载实地实验中，4.0 Mbps主设置下：平均单向延迟从103.0ms降至70.8ms，95百分位延迟从281.2ms降至142.3ms，丢包率从1.7%降至0.8%，平均编码率为0.94。

Conclusion: 调度器无关的自适应FEC方案能在实测车载移动条件下为MPQUIC Datagram带来实际的延迟和可靠性提升，具有良好的实际部署可行性。

Abstract: Multipath transport has long been studied to improve robustness over heterogeneous networks, and Multipath QUIC (MPQUIC) is particularly attractive for low-latency applications because QUIC Datagram enables transmission without retransmissions. However, this advantage comes with a key drawback: QUIC Datagram is vulnerable to packet loss, especially in vehicular cellular environments with handovers and rapidly varying radio conditions. While prior studies have explored adaptive-FEC and coded multipath designs, practical deployment remains challenging when such mechanisms require substantial modifications to the transport stack or scheduler. In this paper, we present an adaptive Forward Error Correction (FEC) scheme for MPQUIC Datagram that reuses QUIC loss detection signals and an off-the-shelf Reed-Solomon (RS) coding library. The sender estimates smoothed per-path loss rates from QUIC loss signals and adaptively determines the number of parity packets for each FEC block according to the expected packet loss. We implement the proposed scheme on an existing MPQUIC stack and evaluate it through vehicular field experiments over three commercial LTE/5G paths. Under the main 4.0 Mbps setting, the proposed scheme improves both reliability and latency compared with No-FEC: the average one-way delay is reduced from 103.0 ms to 70.8 ms, the 95th-percentile delay from 281.2 ms to 142.3 ms, and the packet loss rate from 1.7 % to 0.8 %, with an average coding rate of 0.94. These results indicate that scheduler-agnostic adaptive-FEC can provide practical latency and reliability gains for MPQUIC Datagram under the measured vehicular mobile conditions.

### [270] [Formal Verification for Deep Learning-based Power Control in Massive MIMO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14500)
*Thanh Le,Takeshi Matsumura,Yusheng Ji,John C. S. Lui*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文首次提出形式化验证框架，用于评估深度学习驱动的多小区大规模MIMO系统功率分配算法对输入扰动的鲁棒性，采用DeepPoly抽象传播技术处理非线性约束下的回归问题，实验表明模型可在±1米位置扰动下保持局部鲁棒性且最优性差距不超过1%。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于深度学习的无线通信优化方法虽性能优越，但易受对抗性输入扰动攻击，且当前防御机制缺乏形式化的鲁棒性保证。

Method: 将对抗扰动建模为超矩形约束，采用基于抽象的边界传播技术（DeepPoly）对功率分配输出进行区间界定，并将最小性能需求构建为约束规划问题进行数值可行性分析。

Prior studies on deep learning-based wireless communication optimization have explored supervised learning approaches that map raw user information, such as location or channel state information, to optimal power allocation vectors. While this approach demonstrates competitive performance, it is susceptible to adversarial attacks via input perturbations. Current defense mechanisms primarily rely on empirical methods, which do not provide formal guarantees of robustness. We fill this gap by proposing a formal verification framework to evaluate the robustness of deep learning-based power allocation in multi-cell massive multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) systems against a wide range of potential adversarial input manipulations. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first attempt to formally verify deep neural networks in a regression setting with non-linear output constraints. We model the adversary's capabilities using hyper-rectangle constraints on their perturbation, adopt the abstraction-based bound-propagation technique (DeepPoly) to bound the interval of potential allocated powers, and formulate the minimum performance requirements as a constrained program for numerical feasibility analysis. Evaluation on publicly available datasets for power allocation in multi-cell massive MIMO indicates that a well-trained model can guarantee the local robustness under location perturbation by +-1m while retaining a maximum 1% optimality gap.

</details>


### [271] [Unified Evaluation Methodology for AI-Native Integrated Sensing and Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14806)
*Filip Lemic,Andra Blaga,Francesco Devoti,Guillermo Encinas Lago,Jan Adler,Amitha Mayya,Padmanava Sen,Giorgos Stratidakis,Sotiris Droulias,Angeliki Alexiou,Alexander Artemenko,Aya Mostafa Ahmed,Visa Koivunen,Robin Rajamäki,Simon Schütze,Robert Elschner,Amélie Hennequart,Ahmad Shoukair,Youssef Nasser,Nahuel Soprano-Loto,François Baccelli,Visa Tapio,Paul Almasan,Andra Lutu,Vincenzo Sciancalepore,Carmen Delgado,Xavier Costa-Pérez*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套面向AI原生通感一体化（ISAC）系统的统一架构与评估方法论，包含三阶段验证流程与标准化报告清单，并通过无人机室外与RIS室内两个实例展示如何构建可复现基线，弥合理论研究与部署验证之间的鸿沟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ISAC研究多聚焦波形设计与信道条件，但AI驱动的闭环ISAC系统性能还受推理延迟、不确定性、环境动态及硬件非理想性等因素影响，缺乏统一的评估体系与可复现的对比基线，导致理论增益难以转化为可部署的性能主张。

Method: 提出三阶段验证流水线：(1) 边界与可行性分析；(2) 高保真数字孪生仿真；(3) 初步空口验证。同时设计了从技术KPI（数据率、SINR、检测/跟踪/定位误差、延迟、开销、每决策能耗）到应用层KVI（可用性、任务效能）的标准化报告清单，并通过UAV室外覆盖与RIS室内覆盖两个实例进行具体说明。

Result: 给出了AI原生ISAC系统的统一设计空间形式化描述，构建了涵盖感知-通信-执行闭环的可复现评估框架，并通过两个典型场景展示了如何在不同部署条件下结构化地呈现可比较的实证证据。

Conclusion: 该工作为AI驱动的闭环ISAC系统提供了从理论到验证的完整方法论，有助于推动ISAC领域研究从单项技术突破走向可复现、可比较、可部署的系统级评估。

Abstract: Integrated Sensing and Communication (ISAC) couples radio sensing, data transmission, and control actions within a single closed-loop system. When Artificial Intelligence (AI)-driven policies adapt sensing and communication online across a variety of sensing tasks and objectives, end-to-end performance is shaped not only by waveform and channel conditions but also by inference latency, uncertainty, environmental dynamics, and hardware non-idealities, leading to fundamental trade-offs between sensing accuracy, communication reliability, and resource overhead. This manuscript presents a unified system architecture and evaluation methodology for AI-native ISAC, defined as ISAC in which learning-based agents adapt sensing, communication, and actuation policies online under uncertainty. We formalize the design space of closed-loop ISAC, propose a three-stage validation pipeline from bounds and feasibility analysis, through high-fidelity digital-twin simulation, to preliminary over-the-air validation, and provide a minimal reporting checklist that links technical Key Performance Indicators (KPIs) (e.g., data rate, SINR, target detection, parameter estimation, track quality, localization error, outage, latency, overhead, and energy per decision) to application-level Key Value Indicators (KVIs) (e.g., availability and mission effectiveness). Two representative instantiations, specifically Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV)-based outdoor and Reconfigurable Intelligent Surface (RIS)-enabled indoor coverage extensions, are used to illustrate how to structure reproducible baselines and comparable evidence across heterogeneous deployments, helping bridge the gap between theoretical ISAC gains and deployment-ready performance claims.

</details>


### [272] [Spoofer or Spoofers? Estimating a Lower Bound on the Number of DRDoS Sources Using Anycast Honeypots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14832)
*Bernhard Degen,Bas Palinckx,Mattijs Jonker,Roland van Rijswijk-Deij,Raffaele Sommese*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文通过全球部署的任播放大蜜罐，提出了一种估算参与伪造流量攻击网络数量下限的方法，发现至少21%的DDoS攻击源于多个网络位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DRDoS攻击难以溯源，现有方法无法有效估计攻击者分布的网络数量，亟需一种能够量化攻击分布程度的方法。

Method: 利用全球部署的任播放大蜜罐吸引邻近源请求；基于接收伪造流量的蜜罐集合和TTL值变化构建两种估计器，并考虑自然路径不稳定性。

Result: 分析了287天的放大攻击数据，发现至少21.0%的攻击来源于多个网络位置。

Conclusion: 攻击者经常跨网络分布欺骗活动，对抗欺骗需要协调的分布式防御，该工作为未来溯源技术设计提供了指导。

Abstract: DDoS attacks remain a significant threat, with distributed reflection denial-of-service (DRDoS) attacks being particularly difficult to trace back to their sources. To better understand attacker behavior and deployment patterns, we present a novel approach for estimating a lower bound on the number of networks involved in generating spoofed traffic. Our approach leverages a global deployment of anycast amplification honeypots that attract requests from topologically nearby sources. Using this infrastructure, we develop two estimators based on the set of honeypots receiving spoofed traffic and on variations in observed TTL values, while accounting for natural path instability. Analyzing 287 days of amplification attacks, we find that at least 21.0% originate from multiple network locations, indicating that attackers frequently distribute spoofing activity across networks. Our findings suggest that combating spoofing requires coordinated and distributed defenses, and inform the design of future attribution techniques.

### [273] [Periplus: A Resilient In-band SDN Control Plane via Embedded Forwarding Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14869)
*E. M. Castro Barbero,P. de las Heras Quirós,F. J. Simó Reigadas*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: Periplus是一个面向资源受限广域网的内带SDN控制平面，通过自动引导、源路由和快速故障恢复机制，实现无需全网泛洪的启动、基于图结构的局部故障切换以及亚50毫秒的恢复性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多资源受限的广域网部署能从内带SDN控制平面中受益，但面临着自动引导、源路由、快速故障恢复和多控制器协调等挑战，现有方案难以同时满足这些需求。

Method: Periplus采用三步方法：(1) 引导阶段仅需在两个交换机上安装流规则，避免全网泛洪；(2) 在L2与L3头部之间封装包含主路径和逐跳备选路径的图结构，实现源路由；(3) 交换机沿主路径转发，检测到故障时本地切换到编码备选路径，无需控制器介入。

Result: 基于Ryu和Mininet的实现评估显示：亚50ms的故障恢复时间；跨不同规模和直径拓扑的可扩展引导；每交换机流表条目数与网络规模无关，仅在有多个备选路径的交换机处增长。

Conclusion: Periplus能够在标准Open vSwitch上运行，仅依赖其内置Nicira扩展实现NSH封装，有效解决了资源受限广域网中内带SDN控制平面的关键挑战。

Abstract: Many resource-constrained, wide-area telecommunications deployments could benefit from an in-band SDN control plane, but several challenges stand in the way. This paper presents Periplus, an in-band SDN control plane designed to address four challenges that this approach presents in such contexts: automatic bootstrapping, source-based routing, fast failure recovery, and multi-controller coordination. The first three are developed in detail, while multi-controller coordination is addressed in a separate paper. For bootstrap, Periplus avoids network-wide flooding: when a new switch joins, the controller installs flow rules in only two switches. For routing and failure recovery, Periplus encodes a primary path and per-hop alternatives in a graph structure encapsulated between L2 and L3 headers; switches forward along the primary path and, upon detecting a failure, fall over locally to the encoded alternative without controller involvement. We evaluate a Ryu-based implementation of Periplus in Mininet across multiple topologies. Periplus runs on stock Open vSwitch (OVS), relying only on its built-in Nicira extensions for Network Service Header (NSH) encapsulation. The evaluation shows sub-50 ms failure recovery, scalable bootstrap across topologies of varying size and diameter, and a per-switch flow-table footprint that is independent of network size and grows only at switches where the controller encodes multiple alternatives.

</details>


### [274] [ANet Patu-1: The Value of Connection in the Agent Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15053)
*Mu Yuan,Jinke Song,Zhaomeng Zhou,Lan Zhang*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出ANet Patu-1，一种自组织共识协议，使AI智能体网络在O(1)轮并行共识中自适应地切换于Sarnoff、Metcalfe和Reed三种网络价值定律的上包络线。研究发现：异构弱模型群的集体价值会随规模增长超过同构强模型群（协作缩放律），且异构网络无需设计提示即可自发收敛到ANet Patu-1本身（自反性）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 借鉴互联网网络价值定律（Sarnoff、Metcalfe、Reed），回答AI智能体网络的类似问题：智能体之间的连接如何影响网络价值？以及如何设计最优的协作协议？

Method: 建模协调组大小与网络价值的关系，推导最优协作协议所需属性，提出ANet Patu-1——一种自组织共识协议，网络持续自我重组联盟，以O(1)并行共识轮自适应地运行于三种价值定律的上包络线。

Result: (i) 涌现：异构的弱模型群体在规模增长中集体价值会超越同构的强模型群体，形成协作缩放律；(ii) 自反性：异构网络仅凭自身问题即可自发收敛到ANet Patu-1，重构支配自身连接价值的高维定律。

Conclusion: 智能体网络的协作协议存在最优设计，异构性和自组织能力能使集体智能超越个体能力，且网络可以通过自反过程发现自身的最优连接法则。

Abstract: The Internet taught us that the value of a network depends on \emph{how} its nodes connect: broadcast stars scale as $V\!\propto\!N$ (Sarnoff), fully-connected meshes as $N^2$ (Metcalfe), and group-forming networks as $2^{N}$ (Reed). We ask the analogous question for networks of AI agents. We model the net value of connection as a function of coordination-group size, derive from it the properties an optimal collaboration protocol must have, and introduce ANet Patu-1 -- a self-organizing consensus protocol in which the network continuously re-forms its own coalitions, adaptively riding the upper envelope of all three regimes at $O(1)$ parallel consensus rounds. To measure value without opinion-grading, we score an emergent protocol by formally specifying it and deriving its complexity, the way distributed algorithms are analyzed. Two results follow. (i)~Emergence -- a crowd of the \emph{cheapest} model, when heterogeneous, starts weak but its collective value compounds with $N$ and \emph{overtakes} a crowd of a far \emph{stronger} model that is homogeneous: a crossover that marks a scaling law for collaboration rather than for scale. (ii)~Reflexivity -- a heterogeneous network, given only its own problem and no design hints, converges on ANet Patu-1 itself, reconstructing the high-dimensional law that governs its own connective value.

</details>


### [275] [Adaptive Sampling for Spatiotemporal Anomaly Monitoring in Wireless Sensor Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15235)
*Guoqing Lu,Yixuan Sun,Yiwen Jiang,Bernard Butler*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出一种哨兵辅助自适应采样框架，通过卡尔曼滤波稀疏采样、GLR异常检测和局部警报传播，在无线传感器网络中以较低采样成本实现高异常窗口可见性（AWSR从0.439提升至0.933）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期环境监测中稀疏采样可能遗漏短暂、局部的扩散性异常，现有方法在异常检测与采样成本之间难以取得良好平衡。

Method: 正常时期采用KF预测不确定性驱动的稀疏采样；异常时期持续采样的哨兵节点执行混合GLR检测（节点相对阈值），局部检测触发一跳邻域唤醒与恢复感知的警报控制。

Result: 在Intel Berkeley温度数据集上，AWSR从0.439提升至0.933；相比AAS和Adapted e-Sampling，总成本分别降低15.4%和2.1%。

Conclusion: 融合KF稀疏采样、哨兵GLR检测和局部警报传播可改善异常窗口可见性，同时维持较低的采样-成本权衡。

Abstract: Long-term environmental monitoring in wireless sensor networks (WSNs) often uses sparse sampling to extend network lifetime, but sparse sensing can miss short-lived, localized, and potentially diffusive anomalies. This paper proposes a sentinel-assisted adaptive sampling framework as a cooperative sensing-control pipeline for WSN anomaly monitoring. During normal periods, nodes perform sparse sensing driven by Kalman filter (KF) predictive uncertainty. During anomalous periods, continuously sampled sentinel nodes perform hybrid GLR-based detection with node-relative thresholds, and local detections trigger one-hop neighborhood wake-up with recovery-aware alert control.
  Experiments on the Intel Berkeley Research Lab temperature dataset with abrupt random spatiotemporal anomalies show that the proposed method raises the anomaly-window sampling ratio (AWSR) from 0.439 to 0.933 in the main experiment. It also improves AWSR over Adaptive Data Acquisition with Energy Efficiency and Critical-Sensing Guarantee (AAS) and Adapted e-Sampling while reducing total cost by 15.4\% and 2.1\%, respectively. These results show that integrating KF-based sparse sampling, sentinel GLR detection, and local alert propagation improves anomaly-window visibility while maintaining a lower sampling-cost trade-off.

</details>
